    Perfect — this is clear enough to map **what your current WR already covers** vs **what you still need** for the *agent painkiller wedge* and the later “CRM replacement ladder”.
    
    Below is the **gap map** in plain language, using your WF IDs.
    
    ---
    
    ## **What your current WR already covers (strong coverage)**
    
    ### **The “Viewing Layer” wedge (mostly already there)**
    
    You already have the key building blocks to run the **Pack Link → Book viewing** play:
    
    - **WF-P6 Public Property Page** ✅
        
        This is your “listing page replacement” / the link agents can paste everywhere.
        
    - **WF-H1 Booking Flow** ✅
        
        Booking + buyer gate / SMS verification = strong.
        
    - **WF-O4 Calendar** ✅
        
        Private/group viewings + Google Calendar sync = strong.
        
    - **WF-O3 / WF-H2 Inquiries/Inbox** ✅
        
        Messaging hub exists for both sides.
        
    
    **Bottom line:** You can already deliver the core promise:
    
    **“Book a slot, reduce phone tag, keep it in one place.”**
    
    ---
    
    ## **What’s missing for your**
    
    ## **specific**
    
    ## **“agent painkiller hook” (needs building now)**
    
    These are not “new pages” — they are **behaviours/components** inside existing WFs (fits your rules).
    
    ### **1) Reconfirming + no-show reduction (biggest missing)**
    
    **Where it should live:**
    
    - **WF-H1 Booking Flow** (confirmation step + reminders)
    - **WF-O4 Calendar** (status + auto rules)
    - **WF-A4 Integrations** (WhatsApp/SMS templates + toggles)
    
    **What to add (Phase 1 / Phase 1.5):**
    
    - “Confirm / Reschedule / Cancel” link 24h before viewing
    - optional auto-cancel if not confirmed
    - reminder cadence (e.g., 24h + 2h)
    
    **Why it matters:** this is the pain agents actually feel every day.
    
    ---
    
    ### **2) WhatsApp-style mini questions + explicit consent (your “newsletter fear” killer)**
    
    **Where it should live:**
    
    - **WF-H1 Booking Flow** (a short step before final confirm)
    - **WF-H7 Settings** (preferences & unsubscribe controls)
    
    **What to add:**
    
    - 3 questions max (buy/rent, timeframe, budget band)
    - consent toggles:
        - “Updates about this property only” (default)
        - optional “Weekly digest matching my search” (opt-in)
    
    **Why it matters:** makes agents look premium and reduces junk follow-ups.
    
    ---
    
    ### **3) Post-viewing “still interested?” capture (kills chasing)**
    
    **Where it should live:**
    
    - **WF-H1 / WF-H5** (after viewing prompt)
    - **WF-O1 Dashboard** (shows who is hot/warm/cold)
    - **WF-O3 Inquiries** (status + next action)
    
    **What to add:**
    
    - one-tap feedback: Interested / Maybe / Not for me + reason
    - auto follow-ups based on intent
    
    **Why it matters:** this is literally “two people chasing leads” solved.
    
    ---
    
    ### **4) Agent-friendly “paste everywhere” assets (distribution layer)**
    
    **Where it should live:**
    
    - **WF-O2 My Listings** (generate Pack Link + “portal line” copy)
    - **WF-P6 Public Property Page** (QR + share)
    - **WF-P7 Partners Page** (agent pilot signup)
    
    **What to add:**
    
    - “Copy portal description line”
    - “Copy WhatsApp reply”
    - “QR code for window/flyer”
    - tracking (clicks → bookings)
    
    **Why it matters:** this is how you capture inventory without SEO.
    
    ---
    
    ## **What you already have that supports “CRM replacement later”**
    
    You have a surprisingly strong base for the later ladder:
    
    - **WF-O1 Dashboard** ✅ (can evolve into agent performance + pipeline insights)
    - **WF-O3 Inquiries** ✅ (can become lead triage / tags / templates)
    - **WF-H6 Offers** ✅ (this can become offer management later)
    - **WF-A5 Support** ✅ (can become ops/SLA/task engine)
    - **WF-A4 Integrations** ✅ (key for WhatsApp/SMS/email automation)
    
    **You’re not missing pages. You’re missing:**
    
    - triage statuses,
    - templates,
    - exports,
    - and “rules” (reconfirm, digest, follow-up automation).
    
    ---
    
    ## **Build now vs later (tight list)**
    
    ### **Build now (to win agents fast)**
    
    1. **Reconfirm flow + reminders** (H1 + O4 + A4)
    2. **Mini questions + explicit opt-in** (H1 + H7)
    3. **Post-viewing intent capture** (H1/H5 + O1/O3)
    4. **Pack Link toolset for agents** (O2 + P6)
    
    ### **Build next (to start replacing CRM modules)**
    
    1. **Lead triage inside Inquiries/Inbox** (O3/H2: tags, status, templates)
    2. **Simple pipeline view** (can be a component on O1, not a new page)
    3. **Brochure PDF + CSV export** (inside O2 listing actions)
    
    ### **Build later (deep CRM replacement)**
    
    1. Offer audit trail + negotiation workspace (expand H6)
    2. Team roles + tasks + SLAs (A5→A7 later)
    3. Full reporting and branch management
    
    ---
    
    ## **Quick verdict: are you already MVP-ready for the wedge?**
    
    **Yes** for “book a slot from a link.”
    
    To make it **irresistible for agents**, you need the 3 missing behaviours:
    
    - reconfirm automation,
    - intent capture,
    - consent + digest.
    
    Those three are what converts “nice” into “holy **** this saves us time”.
    
    If you want, I’ll write a **Phase 1.5 spec** (no new pages) listing the exact UI components to add to:
    
    - WF-H1 (Booking)
    - WF-O4 (Calendar)
    - WF-O2 (My Listings)
    - WF-A4 (Integrations)
        
        …with the minimal fields, states, and copy.
        

1. **Move to Phase 2 wedge you care about most:** *Agent-facing “Scheduling + Comms layer”*
    
    That means writing the **Agent Workspace tree** (like you did for Admin) + adding only the minimum screens:
    
    - Agent “Inbox / Enquiries”
    - Agent “Calendar + viewing confirmations”
    - Agent “Listing Pack viewer” (read-only) + “Quote packages”
        
        This is the market-capture wedge.

- Owner Dashbaord details
    
    ## 🎯 Purpose
    
    Owner wireframes define the experience for a person who **lists a place for sale or rent**. This workspace supports everything an Owner must do without an agent: manage places, respond to inquiries, track viewings, review offers, upload documents, and monitor performance.
    
    ---
    
    ## 🛣️ Owner Journey (Short Summary)
    
    **List → Inquiries → Calendar → Offers → Documents → Publish / Update**
    
    1. **List Your Place** — Create a listing in minutes.
    2. **Inquiries** — Respond to home-hunters.
    3. **Calendar** — Manage viewing bookings.
    4. **Offers** — Receive & review offers or applications.
    5. **Documents** — Upload EPC, floorplan, deeds, photos.
    6. **Analytics** — Understand performance.
    7. **Settings** — Manage personal info & integrations.
    8. **Public Property Page** — See how the place appears publicly.
    
    Only **Owner wireframes** are included from this point down. Nothing related to Home-hunters or Admin appears until you request it.
    
    ---
    
    # 🏠 WF-O1 — Owner Dashboard
    
    ## 1. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)
    
    The Owner reaches the Dashboard immediately after logging in or after listing a place.
    
    Journey Position: **Login → Dashboard → My Listings / Inquiries / Calendar**
    
    ## 2. Purpose
    
    Give the Owner an instant overview of performance, activity, and what they should do next.
    
    ## 3. What This Page Should Solve
    
    - Reduce confusion by centralising the most important metrics.
    - Help Owners understand if their place is performing well.
    - Make “next steps” obvious (e.g., update photos, respond to inquiries).
    - Speed up productivity with quick actions.
    
    ## 4. What the Designer Should Build in Framer
    
    - KPI section with cards (Views, Inquiries, Offers)
    - Quick actions panel (List a new place, Arrange a visit)
    - Upcoming viewings section
    - System insights (“Places with fresh photos get more views”)
    - Dashfolio+ dashboard layout with yellow accents
    
    ## 5. Dummy Content (for Designer)
    
    - **Views:** 1,247 this week
    - **Inquiries:** 36
    - **Offers:** 1 active
    - **Upcoming:** “Today 10:00 – Viewing with Sarah L.”
    - **Tip:** “Owners who upload floorplans get 22% more inquiries.”
    
    ---
    
    # 🏢 WF-O2 — My Listings
    
    ## 1. User Journey
    
    Journey Position: **Dashboard → My Listings → Edit / Preview / Publish**
    
    Owners spend most of their time here managing their places.
    
    ## 2. Purpose
    
    Give Owners a clear overview of all places they have listed.
    
    ## 3. What This Page Should Solve
    
    - Help Owners quickly update photos, descriptions, and prices.
    - Make it easy to publish or unpublish a place.
    - Provide visibility on performance (views, status).
    
    ## 4. What the Designer Should Build in Framer
    
    - Table or card layout with: Place · Status · Price · Views
    - Action buttons: Edit · Preview · Publish
    - Yellow CTA: “List a new place”
    - Hover states in light gray (Dashfolio+)
    
    ## 5. Dummy Content
    
    Example row:
    
    - **12 King Street** — Live — £650,000 — 523 views — ✏ Edit · 🔗 Preview
    - **45 Oak Road** — Draft — £410,000 — — 🚀 Publish
    
    ---
    
    # 💬 WF-O3 — Inquiries (Messages)
    
    ## 1. User Journey
    
    Journey Position: **My Listings → Inquiry Notification → Inquiries Page**
    
    ## 2. Purpose
    
    Provide a unified messaging hub for direct communication with Home-hunters.
    
    ## 3. What This Page Should Solve
    
    - Reduce message chaos scattered across portals.
    - Help Owners respond quickly and professionally.
    - Allow filtering (new, replied, offers).
    
    ## 4. What the Designer Should Build
    
    - Two-column layout: Inbox left, Conversation right.
    - Filters at top.
    - Message bubbles in a dark theme.
    - AI reply suggestions in yellow.
    
    ## 5. Dummy Content
    
    Inbox:
    
    - **Sarah L.** — “Is the kitchen newly renovated?” (12 King Street)
    - **Omar R.** — “Could I book a viewing this weekend?” (45 Oak Road)
        
        Conversation example reply:
        
        “Hi Sarah, yes — the kitchen was fully renovated in 2023. Would you like the floorplan?”
        
    
    ---
    
    # 📊 WF-O4 — Analytics
    
    ## 1. User Journey
    
    Journey Position: **Dashboard → Analytics**
    
    ## 2. Purpose
    
    Provide Owners with performance insights that help them improve their listing.
    
    ## 3. What This Page Should Solve
    
    - Show whether a place is performing well.
    - Help identify where inquiries are coming from.
    - Show drop-off points in the funnel.
    
    ## 4. Designer Instructions
    
    - Funnel: Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Offers
    - Source charts: Yalla.House, Rightmove, Zoopla, etc.
    - A graph of views over time.
    - Highlight top-performing place.
    
    ## 5. Dummy Content
    
    - **Views:** 4,562 (last 30 days)
    - **Inquiries:** 123
    - **Viewings:** 17
    - **Offers:** 3
    - **Top Source:** Yalla.House (45%)
    - **Top Place:** 12 King Street (612 views)
    
    ---
    
    # 📁 WF-O5 — Documents
    
    ## 1. User Journey
    
    Journey Position: **My Listings → Documents**
    
    ## 2. Purpose
    
    Provide a secure place for Owners to upload essential documents.
    
    ## 3. What This Page Should Solve
    
    - Avoid document confusion.
    - Ensure visibility of EPC and floorplan.
    - Allow public/private control.
    
    ## 4. Designer Instructions
    
    - Table layout of files
    - “Upload new document” CTA
    - Drag & drop zone
    - Public/private toggle (yellow)
    
    ## 5. Dummy Content
    
    - **EPC_Certificate.pdf** — Public — 04 Nov 2025
    - **Floorplan.png** — Public — 02 Nov 2025
    - **OwnershipProof.pdf** — Private — 30 Oct 2025
    
    ---
    
    # 📅 WF-O6 — Calendar
    
    ## 1. User Journey
    
    Journey Position: **Dashboard → Calendar**
    
    ## 2. Purpose
    
    Help Owners manage viewings and callbacks.
    
    ## 3. What This Page Should Solve
    
    - Make availability clear.
    - Avoid double-booking.
    - Keep track of all viewings.
    
    ## 4. Designer Instructions
    
    - Monthly calendar grid
    - Days with events in yellow
    - Right agenda panel
    - Add event button
    - Integrate visually with Dashfolio
    
    ## 5. Dummy Content

    - **10:00 AM** – Viewing (12 King Street, Sarah L.)
    - **4:00 PM** – Callback (Omar R.)

    ---
    
    ## 1. User Journey
    
    **My Listings → Preview Public Page**
    
    Visitors arrive mainly from search, share links, WhatsApp, or confirmation emails.
    
    This page determines whether the visitor **books a visit**, **sends a message**, or **submits an offer**.
    
    ---
    
    ## 2. Purpose
    
    To present the place in a **trustworthy, modern, conversion-first** way.
    
    The primary goal is to make **Arrange a Visit** the most prominent, frictionless action.
    
    ---
    
    ## 3. What This Page Should Solve
    
    - Clear and structured presentation of information
    - Very easy viewing booking (always visible)
    - Quick contact + offer pathways
    - High trust: floorplan, EPC, map, documents
    - Ability to highlight extra selling points (extensions, local area)
    
    ---
    
    ## 4. Designer Instructions (Framer Build)
    
    ### A. Hero Section
    
    - Large photo gallery (carousel)
    - Optional video tour
    - Status badge overlay: **For Sale / Under Offer / Sold**
    
    ### B. Primary Actions
    
    - **Arrange a Visit** (Primary CTA – Yalla Yellow)
    - **Message Owner** (Secondary CTA)
    - **Make an Offer** (Optional for MVP)
    
    ### C. Booking CTA Placement — MUST APPEAR IN 3 SPOTS
    
    1. Inside Hero block
    2. Sticky CTA on scroll (top or bottom)
    3. Right‑hand info panel (desktop)
    
    ### D. Details Block
    
    - Title
    - Sale Price
    - Address
    - Status badge
    - **Online Since** (optional highlight)
    - Features (Beds, Baths, Size, Outdoor Space)
    
    ### E. Description Block
    
    Long‑form descriptive text about the place.
    
    ### F. Additional Optional Sections
    
    - **Extension Potential**
    - **Neighbourhood Snapshot** (transport, schools, local shops)
    
    ### G. Floorplan + Documents
    
    - Floorplan preview
    - EPC + other documents
    - Only public files shown
    
    ### H. Map Section
    
    - Google Maps embed OR image placeholder
    
    ### I. Sticky CTA on Scroll
    
    - Arrange a Visit (yellow)
    - Message Owner
    - Make an Offer (if active)
    
    ### J. Footer: About Yalla.House
    
    Short text e.g.:
    
    “Yalla.House helps Owners connect directly with Home‑hunters — no commission, no agents, full transparency.”
    
    ---
    
    ## 5. Integrations (Developer Notes)
    
    ### Booking Calendar
    
    - Sync with Owner’s Google Calendar
    - Show available times dynamically
    - Block unavailable times
    - Auto-send confirmation email with visit details
    
    ### Messaging System
    
    - Internal inbox (WF‑O3)
    - Optional WhatsApp integration via Twilio
    
    ### Offer System
    
    - Optional for MVP
    - When enabled, show **Make an Offer** button
    - Creates an offer record in Owner dashboard
    
    ### Documents
    
    - Pulled from Owner Documents (WF‑O5)
    - Only documents marked PUBLIC appear here
    
    ### Analytics Tracking
    
    Track:
    
    - Page view
    - Visit CTA click
    - Message Owner click
    - Offer click (if enabled)
    - Document downloads
    - Image/gallery interactions

## **User Research**

**Purpose:**

Validate our assumptions about sellers and buyers so NoAgent builds only what truly matters: **trust, simplicity, and control.**

Each study = one hypothesis → one insight → one decision.

---

### **📊 Dashboard**

**Overview Table (example):**

| **Study** | **Hypothesis** | **Method** | **Status** | **Key Insight** | **Action** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Seller onboarding flow | Sellers want a short form — they’ll abandon if it takes over 2 minutes | Observation / Survey | 🔄 In Progress | TBD | Simplify form, test auto-fill |
| Buyer communication | Buyers trust direct chat more than agent mediation | Interview | ✅ Complete | True for 7/10 | Keep direct chat in MVP |
| Pricing transparency | Sellers underestimate hidden fees | Survey | ✅ Complete | Confirmed | Keep “No Fees. No Commission.” headline |

---

### **👩‍💼 Seller Research**

**Goal:** Understand how sellers think, decide, and act when selling without agents.

| **Hypothesis** | **Method** | **Result Summary** | **Next Step** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Sellers fear legal paperwork more than marketing | Interviews | ✅ Confirmed – “Contracts scare me.” | Integrate contract templates / legal partner |
| Sellers mainly care about speed, not savings | Survey (n=20) | ❌ Rejected – Savings ranked #1 | Keep “Save £X” front and centre |
| Sellers will pay small fixed fee if process feels safe | Offer mock test | 🟡 Mixed – 50/50 interest | Test trust badges & refund policy |

---

### **🏡 Buyer Research**

**Goal:** Learn what drives buyers to engage directly and what creates trust.

| **Hypothesis** | **Method** | **Result Summary** | **Next Step** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Buyers prefer messaging sellers directly | Interviews | ✅ True – faster and more personal | Keep direct chat as a core MVP feature |
| Buyers expect agent-style viewing scheduling | Survey | 🟡 Partial | Build optional guided booking calendar |
| Buyers are cautious about scams | Observation | ✅ Confirmed | Add “Verified Listing” label + safety FAQ |

---

### **📋 Quick Study Template**

**Title:** [User Type] – [Topic] – [Date]

**Hypothesis:**

> We believe that [user group] wants [behaviour/outcome] because [reason].
> 

**Method:** Interview / Survey / Prototype Test

**Participants:** [# and type]

**Result Summary:** True / False / Mixed

**Key Quotes:** “I just want to know who’s serious.”

**Next Step:** [Decision or design action]

---

### **🧩 Insights Board**

| **Theme** | **Evidence** | **Action** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Trust | 9/10 sellers mentioned fear of scams | Build verified ID flow |
| Time | Sellers want fewer clicks | Streamline photo upload |
| Control | Buyers want choice of contact channel | Keep chat + email options |

---

### **⚙️ Suggested Notion Setup**

Create **three databases** in Notion:

1. **Studies** → Properties: Hypothesis, Method, Status, Result, Action
2. **Insights** → Tags: Seller / Buyer / Trust / Pricing
3. **Decisions** → Link to product roadmap

Each entry ends with one summary line:

> Finding:
> 

> Action:
>

## **Traditional Real Estate Agent – Full Job Breakdown**

### **⚙️ Overview**

Estate agents act as **intermediaries** between sellers and buyers. They handle **marketing, viewings, negotiations, paperwork**, and coordination with **solicitors, mortgage brokers, and surveyors** until completion.

They charge **1–3% commission** of the sale price (often £3,000–£10,000+).

---

## **🧩 1. Seller Onboarding & Valuation**

| **Step** | **Description** | **Effort** | **Automatable?** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Initial contact / lead intake** | Seller calls or fills out form; agent qualifies property type, motivation, and timeline. | Low (15–30 min) | ✅ Yes – online forms, auto-CRM entry |
| **Property valuation visit** | Agent visits, inspects, researches comparables, sets listing price. | High (1–2 hrs) | ⚙️ Partially – use AI + data comparables, automate estimate |
| **Proposal & contract signing** | Agent sends agency agreement (sole agency / multi-agency). | Medium | ✅ Digital contract + e-signature |
| **ID & AML checks** | Seller identity verification (passport, proof of address). | Medium | ✅ Automated via KYC provider (eg. Sumsub, Onfido) |

---

## **📸 2. Property Preparation & Marketing**

| **Step** | **Description** | **Effort** | **Automatable?** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Professional photos & floorplan** | Arrange photographer / measure rooms. | Medium | ⚙️ Partially – seller self-upload or integrated booking |
| **EPC certificate** | Arrange Energy Performance Certificate (legal requirement). | Low | ⚙️ Auto-book via partner network |
| **Property description writing** | Create copy for listings. | Medium | ✅ AI-generate based on form data |
| **Listing on portals (Rightmove, Zoopla, OTM)** | Upload details and verify compliance. | Medium | ✅ API integration with portals |
| **Marketing materials** | Brochures, social media posts, ads. | Medium | ✅ Automated templates & scheduling tools |

---

## **👀 3. Buyer Engagement**

| **Step** | **Description** | **Effort** | **Automatable?** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Lead capture** | Collect enquiries via portals, calls, walk-ins. | High (manual responses) | ✅ CRM lead capture + auto-reply |
| **Screening buyers** | Check financial status, mortgage in principle, seriousness. | Medium | ⚙️ Online buyer pre-qualification form |
| **Scheduling viewings** | Coordinate time between seller & buyer. | High (lots of back-and-forth) | ✅ Calendar sync & auto-booking |
| **Conducting viewings** | Show property, highlight features, answer questions. | High | ❌ No – unless seller self-hosts or uses 3D tours |
| **Follow-up & feedback** | Collect buyer feedback & report to seller. | Medium | ✅ Automated feedback form & dashboard |

---

## **💬 4. Negotiation & Offer Handling**

| **Step** | **Description** | **Effort** | **Automatable?** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Offer submission** | Buyer submits offer, sometimes verbally. | Medium | ✅ Structured offer form with verification |
| **Negotiation** | Discuss price, conditions, timing with both sides. | High | ⚙️ Partially – suggest counter-offers algorithmically |
| **Offer acceptance confirmation** | Notify all parties, issue Memorandum of Sale. | Medium | ✅ Auto-generate MoS once offer accepted |

---

## **🧾 5. Legal Progression (Conveyancing)**

| **Step** | **Description** | **Effort** | **Automatable?** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Solicitor coordination** | Exchange details between buyer & seller solicitors. | Medium | ✅ Automated data transfer |
| **Draft contract & searches** | Solicitors handle local searches, contracts, etc. | High (weeks of work) | ❌ No – human legal review required |
| **Mortgage & survey liaison** | Buyer’s lender/surveyor contacts agent for access. | Medium | ⚙️ Calendar integration possible |
| **Chain management** | Update on dependencies (if seller also buying). | High | ⚙️ Automated progress tracker updates |
| **Exchange of contracts** | Buyer pays deposit; completion date fixed. | High | ❌ Legal step – must be solicitor-led |
| **Completion** | Funds transferred; keys released. | Medium | ⚙️ Partial – notification automation possible |

---

## **🧮 6. Post-Sale & Aftercare**

| **Step** | **Description** | **Effort** | **Automatable?** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Key handover** | Buyer collects keys or locks changed. | Low | ✅ Pickup verification / smart lock |
| **Commission invoicing** | Agent issues invoice to solicitor. | Low | ✅ Automated billing |
| **Customer review request** | Collect testimonial. | Low | ✅ Automated email sequence |
| **Referral network** | Recommend removals, utilities, insurance. | Medium | ✅ Affiliate marketplace integration |

---

# **🔍 Summary Table – What Can Be Automated**

| **Category** | **% Automatable** | **Main Tools/Systems** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Seller onboarding | 90% | Google Form + e-signature + CRM |
| Marketing setup | 80% | AI text + image upload + portal API |
| Buyer engagement | 70% | CRM + auto-calendar + feedback form |
| Negotiation & offers | 60% | Offer platform + AI suggestion |
| Conveyancing | 40% | Legal workflow + updates only |
| Completion & aftercare | 90% | Notification + referral system |

---

# **⚡**

# **Key NoAgent Automation Opportunities**

✅ Online seller intake form → auto-generate listing

✅ Auto-valuation & AI-generated description

✅ Automated photo booking & EPC partner link

✅ API posting to Rightmove, Zoopla, OTM

✅ Buyer CRM with auto-reply, viewing booking & feedback

✅ Digital negotiation & offer forms

✅ Real-time legal progress tracker (via solicitor integration)

✅ Optional human concierge layer (for sellers who want assistance)

---

# **🧠 Typical Effort in Traditional Model**

| **Stage** | **Time (hours)** | **Human interaction** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Valuation + listing | 4–6 hrs | In-person visit |
| Marketing & updates | 2–3 hrs | Calls, uploads |
| Viewings | 5–10 hrs | Repeated showings |
| Negotiation | 1–3 hrs | Calls, emails |
| Conveyancing follow-up | 5–15 hrs | Weeks of chasing |
| **Total** | **20–35 hrs per property** | **≈ 50–60 human touchpoints** |

---

Would you like me to now **map this checklist to a NoAgent flow** (showing what’s replaced by automation, what’s optional concierge, and what’s solicitor-only)?

That would give a clear **“Before vs After NoAgent”** comparison — perfect for your investor deck or MVP documentation.

## **🧭 NoAgent vs Traditional Estate Agent – Full Automation Map**

| **Stage** | **Traditional Estate Agent Task** | **Effort / Cost** | **Pain Points** | **NoAgent Automation / Replacement** | **Human Needed?** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **1️⃣ Seller Onboarding** | In-person valuation visit | 1–2 hrs | Subjective, commission-driven | ✅ AI + data-driven valuation (Zoopla, Land Registry, AI pricing tool) | Optional human check |
|  | Manual contract signing | 30 min | Paperwork, delays | ✅ Digital agreement via e-sign | ❌ |
|  | ID & AML checks | 20 min | Manual checks, delays | ✅ KYC integration (Onfido/Sumsub) | ❌ |
|  | Data entry into CRM | 30 min | Manual, error-prone | ✅ Auto-fill from intake form | ❌ |
| **→ Result:** Seller listed same day instead of days/weeks |  |  |  |  |  |

---

| **2️⃣ Property Preparation & Marketing** | Arrange photography | 1 hr | Coordination, delays | ✅ Partner booking link or self-upload | Optional |

| | Order EPC | 1 hr | Coordination | ✅ Auto-book via integrated partners | ❌ |

| | Write property description | 45 min | Subjective & inconsistent | ✅ AI-generated listing text | ❌ |

| | Upload listing to Rightmove/Zoopla/OTM | 1–2 hrs | Manual uploads | ✅ FeedSync / PropertyHive integration | ❌ |

| | Marketing materials | 1 hr | Manual templates | ✅ Auto-design with Canva/API | ❌ |

| **→ Result:** Property live in <24h vs 3–5 days |  |  |  |  |  |

---

| **3️⃣ Buyer Engagement** | Capture & reply to enquiries | Continuous | Repetitive & inconsistent | ✅ Auto-confirmation + lead capture form + CRM tagging | ❌ |

| | Schedule viewings | 2–4 hrs | Back-and-forth emails | ✅ Calendar sync (Google, Calendly) | Optional |

| | Conduct viewings | Several hours | Human required | ⚙️ Seller self-showings / 3D virtual tour | ✅ |

| | Collect feedback | 30 min | Often forgotten | ✅ Automated form sent after viewing | ❌ |

| | Update seller | 30 min | Manual | ✅ Seller dashboard with live updates | ❌ |

| **→ Result:** Zero missed leads, faster follow-up, instant transparency |  |  |  |  |  |

---

| **4️⃣ Negotiation & Offers** | Handle offers manually | 1–2 hrs | Miscommunication risk | ✅ Buyer offer form + auto-notify seller | ❌ |

| | Negotiate terms | 1–2 hrs | Emotional / biased | ⚙️ AI-assisted counter-offer suggestion | Optional |

| | Create Memorandum of Sale | 30 min | Manual template | ✅ Auto-generated on acceptance | ❌ |

| **→ Result:** Faster & traceable offer handling |  |  |  |  |  |

---

| **5️⃣ Legal Progression (Conveyancing)** | Send solicitor details | 20 min | Email delays | ✅ Auto-share via dashboard | ❌ |

| | Chase solicitor progress | Weeks | Time drain | ⚙️ Solicitor API / status tracking (buyer/seller both see) | ❌ |

| | Handle surveyor access | 30 min | Calls/emails | ✅ Auto-booking link | Optional |

| | Manage completion chain | 1–2 hrs | Manual | ⚙️ Chain progress dashboard | Optional |

| **→ Result:** Transparency + less chasing |  |  |  |  |  |

---

| **6️⃣ Post-Sale & Aftercare** | Release keys | 30 min | Manual pickup | ⚙️ Smart key box / pickup code | Optional |

| | Send invoice | 10 min | Paper/email | ✅ Auto-invoicing | ❌ |

| | Request reviews | 15 min | Low response | ✅ Automated review campaign | ❌ |

| | Offer partner referrals | 30 min | Manual | ✅ Automated partner marketplace (removals, insurance, etc.) | ❌ |

| **→ Result:** Ongoing engagement + passive revenue |  |  |  |  |  |

---

# **⚡At a Glance – Automation Impact**

| **Area** | **Traditional Time** | **With NoAgent** | **Automation Potential** | **Commission/Cost Saved** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Seller onboarding | 3 hrs | 20 min | 90% | £500+ |
| Marketing setup | 5 hrs | 1 hr | 80% | £1000+ |
| Buyer engagement | 6 hrs | 1 hr | 85% | £2000+ |
| Offers & negotiation | 3 hrs | 30 min | 80% | £1000+ |
| Legal progression | 10–15 hrs | 2 hrs (monitoring only) | 70% | £1000+ |
| Aftercare | 2 hrs | 15 min | 90% | £500+ |
| **TOTAL** | **≈30 hrs per sale** | **≈4–5 hrs** | **≈85% reduction** | **Save £5k–£10k avg per sale** |

---

# **💡 NoAgent Product Modules (Mapped to Automation)**

| **Module** | **Purpose** | **Replaces** | **Tech Stack Suggestion** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Seller Intake Form | Gather property data, ID, pricing goals | Agent intake call | Google Form + Sheets CRM |
| Auto-Valuation Engine | Suggests price using AI comparables | In-person valuation | Zoopla API + Land Registry data |
| Listing Builder | Creates text, images, floorplans | Manual upload | Webflow/Framer + FeedSync |
| Buyer CRM | Centralises buyer enquiries | Manual follow-up | Airtable/Glide dashboard |
| Viewings Scheduler | Connects buyers/sellers directly | Agent diaries | Google Calendar + Calendly |
| Offer Platform | Tracks offers, generates MoS | Agent negotiations | Custom Airtable form |
| Conveyancing Tracker | Displays solicitor progress | Phone/email chasing | Shared dashboard / integration |
| Referral Marketplace | Monetise after-sale services | Manual referrals | Affiliate widget / Notion database |

- **WF-A1-A9 Wireframes & UX ( Admin)**(internal control tools)
    - **WF-A1 — Admin Dashboard (System Command Center)**
        
        This is the *central hub* for all Admin/Founder operations.
        
        No canvas. Plain text. Clean. Ready to paste into Notion.
        
        ---
        
        # **Audience:** Founder + Admin (NOT visible to Support)
        
        **Purpose:** Real-time operational intelligence and early warnings.
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣ Designer Checklist**
        
        **Layout & UX**
        
        - Dark Dashfolio+ style (unchanged)
        - 2-column grid:
            - LEFT = Metrics + System Health
            - RIGHT = Alerts + Tasks
        - Sticky header with:
            - “Admin Dashboard”
            - Role badge (Founder/Admin)
        - Quick-filter tabs:
            - **Overview | Owners | Buyers | Support | Integrations**
        - Charts simple, beautiful, readable on mobile + desktop
        - Everything collapsible for smaller screens
        - Use Yalla Yellow highlights for:
            - warnings
            - low performance
            - actions needed
        
        **Components Needed**
        
        - KPI cards
        - Inline charts (bar, line, pie)
        - Table components
        - “Flagged Issues” list
        - “AI Recommendations” block
        - “System Health Lights” (green/orange/red)
        
        ---
        
        # **2️⃣ Developer Checklist**
        
        **Data required**
        
        - Owners table
        - Buyers table
        - Listings table
        - Inquiries table
        - Portal sync logs
        - Twilio logs
        - Support tickets
        - Calendar bookings
        - Photos/EPC orders
        - Errors & warnings
        - All KPIs are calculated from analytics_events + billing aggregates.
        
        **APIs to wire**
        
        - Stripe revenue (monthly + MRR)
        - Twilio usage
        - Portal sync status (Rightmove, Zoopla, OTM)
        - Internal analytics endpoint
        - Survey marketplace
        - Support inbox feed
        
        **Security**
        
        - Only Admin + Founder allowed
        - All sensitive data masked for Admin (unmask button, logged)
        - Audit trail on every interaction
        
        **Performance**
        
        - Cache metrics every 10 min
        - Render charts from cached JSON
        - Error logs real-time
        
        ---
        
        # **3️⃣ User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
        
        Admin Dashboard is the first page after login for:
        
        - **Founders**
        - **Admin/Operations staff**
        
        It is NOT visible to:
        
        - Support staff
        - Buyers
        - Owners
        - Developers (unless granted view-only)
        
        This is the **starting point** for all administration tasks.
        
        ---
        
        # **4️⃣ Purpose of WF-A1**
        
        This page tells you, at a glance:
        
        - How the business is performing
        - Which owners need help
        - Which buyers need verification
        - What integrations are failing
        - What tasks must be done today
        - What survey opportunities exist
        - What churn risks exist
        - What revenue and cost projections look like
        
        In short:
        
        > WF-A1 is your operational nerve center.
        > 
        
        ---
        
        # **5️⃣ What This Page Should Solve**
        
        ✔ Show **real-time business health**
        
        ✔ Flag **problems early** (e.g., Rightmove sync broken)
        
        ✔ Highlight **owners at risk of churn**
        
        ✔ Show **buyers needing verification**
        
        ✔ Show **profitability at a glance**
        
        ✔ Centralise **operational tasks**
        
        ✔ Provide **AI recommendations**
        
        ✔ Allow Manager to assign tasks
        
        ✔ Give Founders a high-level pulse check
        
        ---
        
        # **6️⃣ What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
        
        ### **6.1 Layout Overview**
        
        - **Hero Row:**
            
            4 KPI cards
            
            - Active Owners
            - Active Places
            - MRR (Monthly Recurring Revenue)
            - Viewings Booked (7 days)
        - **Section 2: Revenue & Costs**
            - MRR line chart (30 days)
            - Revenue breakdown pie chart
            - Cost breakdown pie chart
            - “Net margin” badge
        - **Section 3: Performance Heatmap**
            - Table with color-coded performance for each owner:
                - Views
                - Inquiries
                - Viewings
                - Offers
                - Rating
        - **Section 4: Critical Alerts** (Red/Yellow)
            - Rightmove sync failures
            - Twilio delivery issues
            - Portal errors
            - Listings stuck in draft
            - Owners not replying
        - **Section 5: Today’s Tasks**
            - Signs to deliver
            - Photos to schedule
            - EPC pending
            - Verification pending
            - Escalated support tickets
        - **Section 6: AI Recommendations**
            - Pricing suggestions
            - Upsell opportunities
            - Churn-risk owners
            - Survey to purchase
            - SEO boost suggestions
        - **Section 7: System Health Panel**
            - Lights (Green/Yellow/Red)
            - Portals
            - WhatsApp
            - Calendar
            - Payments
            - Hosting
        
        ---
        
        # **7️⃣ Developer Requirements**
        
        ### **Data endpoints**
        
        - /admin/kpis
        - /admin/owners/heatmap
        - /admin/alerts
        - /admin/tasks
        - /admin/recommendations
        - /admin/system-health
        - /portal/sync-status
        
        ### **Authentication**
        
        - Only **Admin** and **Founder** can access
        - Must use JWT + Role middleware
        - Support session timeout + MFA for founders
        
        ### **Data masking**
        
        - Email, phone masked:
            - e.g. ta***@gmail.com
            - Show full only when clicked (logged)
        
        ### **Error handling**
        
        - Surface last 10 critical errors
        - Retry option for portal syncs
        - Show error codes with timestamp
        
        ---
        
        # **8️⃣ KPI Definitions (Precise)**
        
        | **KPI** | **Definition** | **Source** |
        | --- | --- | --- |
        | **Active Owners** | Owners with ≥1 active listing OR onboarding status >20% | Owner table |
        | **Active Places** | Listings in “Live,” “Under Offer,” or “Let Agreed” | Listings table |
        | **MRR** | Sum of monthly subscriptions (minus Stripe fee) | Stripe API |
        | **Bookings (7d)** | Number of calendar bookings | Calendar events |
        
        Additional:
        
        - **Owner Health Score** = avg response time + progress + engagement
        - **Buyer Verification Queue** = pending ID checks
        - **Survey Profit** = survey sales – cost
        
        ---
        
        # **9️⃣ Conversion Funnel (Global)**
        
        ```
        Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Offers → Sale/Rent
        ```
        
        With global funnel percentages on dashboard:
        
        - Global CTR (views → inquiry)
        - Global conversion (inquiry → viewing)
        - Offer conversion (viewing → offer)
        - Sale conversion (offer → accepted)
        
        ---
        
        # **🔟 Business Cost Calculation**
        
        Displayed on dashboard:
        
        ```
        Portal cost (active listings × per-listing cost)
        Twilio cost (messages × rate)
        Map cost (loads × rate)
        AI cost (tokens × rate)
        Support cost (minutes × internal rate)
        Total monthly overhead (manual input)
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **🔁 AI Recommendations Engine (Admin Dashboard)**
        
        Examples shown:
        
        - “Owner Maria F. has 3 unanswered inquiries.”
        - “Price reduction recommended for 12 Oak Road.”
        - “Order sign for 19 Hill Drive (high foot traffic).”
        - “Consider buying survey for 88 Rose Lane (£250 → £900 potential).”
        - “Rightmove feed unstable, 3 listings not updated.”
        
        ---
        
        # **🗂 System Health Panel**
        
        Green/Yellow/Red for:
        
        - Rightmove feed
        - Zoopla feed
        - WhatsApp API
        - Calendar API
        - Stripe payments
        - Hosting uptime
        - Database health

        # **🔥 30-Second Summary for Developers**
        
        “Admin Dashboard aggregates all business data: owners, buyers, listings, revenue, costs, tasks, alerts, and system health. It must be role-protected, cached for performance, and include real-time error logs and recommendations. Use modular endpoints (/admin/*), implement masking, and show KPI cards, charts, heatmaps, and a task manager. This page is the central command center for founders and admin-level staff.”

        # **🌐 Admin Sitemap Connection**
        
        WF-A1 connects to:
        
        → **WF-A2 Owner Detail** (click on any owner from heatmap)
        
        → **WF-A3 Integrations & Logs** (click on system errors)
        
        → **WF-A4 Tasks & Fulfillment** (click on task list)
        
        → **WF-A5 Buyer Detail** (pending verification list)

    - **WF-A2 Owner Detail View (Admin + Founder)**
        
        ---
        
        **Audience:** Founder + Admin (Support has a lighter version)
        
        **Purpose:** Give a 360° view of an Owner and their listing(s).
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣ Designer Checklist**
        
        - Follow Dashfolio+ dark theme
        - 2-column layout (main info left, side widgets right)
        - Sections are collapsible
        - Sensitive fields masked by default
        - Tabs or sections for:
            - Overview
            - Listings
            - Inquiries
            - Viewings
            - Revenue & Cost
            - Surveys
            - Behaviour Signals
            - AI Recommendations
        - Buttons:
            - “Message Owner”
            - “View Listing”
            - “Impersonate Owner (Founder-only)”
            - “Create Task”
        - Highlight:
            - Problems (yellow)
            - Critical (red)
            - Good performance (green)
        
        ---
        
        # **2️⃣ Developer Checklist**
        
        - Requires Admin or Founder token
        - Sensitive data masked by default
        - Endpoints needed:
        
        ```
        /admin/owner/:id
        /admin/owner/:id/listings
        /admin/owner/:id/inquiries
        /admin/owner/:id/viewings
        /admin/owner/:id/financials
        /admin/owner/:id/surveys
        /admin/owner/:id/recommendations
        /admin/tasks/create
        ```
        
        - Must log every:
            - “View full email/phone”
            - “Send message”
            - “Impersonate owner”
        - Cache non-sensitive data (listing stats)
        - Real-time for:
            - Inquiries
            - Errors
            - Messages
        - Full GDPR pseudonymisation when “Support view”
        
        ---
        
        # **3️⃣ Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
        
        This WF shows where the Owner is in their journey:
        
        ```
        Signed up → Started Listing → Published → Accepting Viewings →
        Replying to buyers → Offers → Sold/Rented → Offboarded
        ```
        
        Admin sees:
        
        - % completion of onboarding
        - Where the owner got stuck
        - Whether they need help
        - Their responsiveness
        - What’s blocking offers
        
        ---
        
        # **4️⃣ User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
        
        WF-A2 loads when Admin clicks:
        
        - Owner name from Admin Dashboard
        - Listing heatmap
        - Support ticket related to owner
        - Integrations error tied to a listing
        
        This page replaces a CRM — it’s the **Owner cockpit**.
        
        ---
        
        # **5️⃣ Purpose**
        
        WF-A2 answers:
        
        ### **✨ “How is this owner doing — operationally, financially, performance-wise, and behaviourally?”**
        
        It enables Admin/Founder to:
        
        - identify problems
        - support the owner
        - optimise performance
        - monitor profitability
        - see risk of churn
        - see errors affecting that listing
        - manage documents
        - check buyer inquiries
        - assess whether this user is profitable or costly

        # **9️⃣ KPI Definitions (Specific to Owner)**
        
        | **KPI** | **Meaning** |
        | --- | --- |
        | **Engagement Score** | Logins, replies, edits |
        | **Owner Health Score** | Liveness signal |
        | **Churn Risk** | % probability of leaving |
        | **Demand Score** | Views vs expected |
        | **Funnel Conversion** | Inquiry → viewing → offer |
        | **Profit per Owner** | Revenue – Costs |
        | **Support Time** | Minutes spent helping |
        | **Operational Load** | How much admin work needed |

        ```
        Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Offers → Deal Done
        ```
        
        Color-coded:
        
        - Green = outperforming area
        - Yellow = average
        - Red = underperforming

        # **1️⃣1️⃣ Survey Logic**
        
        Each listing stores:
        
        ```
        surveyStatus: none / uploaded / shared / purchased
        surveyCost: number
        surveySalePrice: number
        surveyMargin: calculated automatically
        surveyBuyRecommendation: yes/no
        ```

        # **1️⃣2️⃣ Developer Tooling Overview (For This Page)**
        
        Integrations needed:
        
        - Stripe revenue
        - Twilio logs
        - Portal feed log
        - Calendar API
        - Map API
        - AI scoring service
        - Internal analytics engine
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣3️⃣ Dummy Content (Copy Example)**
        
        **Owner:** “Sarah Johnson”
        
        **Email:** sa***@gmail.com
        
        **Phone:** 07*** 992 301
        
        **Plan:** Pro
        
        **Listing:** 12 King Street
        
        **Views (7d):** 623
        
        **Inquiries:** 18
        
        **Viewings:** 4
        
        **Offers:** 1 (£517,000)
        
        **Revenue total:** £312
        
        **Costs total:** £48
        
        **Net margin:** 84%
        
        **AI alert:**
        
        > “Price is 4% above local range. Reduce £5,000 to increase inquiries by 18–25%.”
        > 
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣4️⃣  Rental Logic (Integrated)**
        
        If listing = Rent:
        
        Replace:
        
        - Asking Price → Rent per month
        - Tenure removed
        - Deposit added
        - Minimum Term added
        
        Add:
        
        - EPC rating (mandatory in rental flow)
        - Compliance warnings (unfurnished/furnished)
        - “No smoking / no pets” tags
        
        Admin sees:
        
        - Average rent in area
        - Rent ranking
        - Tenant inquiries visible
        - Compliance missing (safety certs, EPC)
        
        ---
        
        # **⚡️ 30-Second Dev Summary**
        
        “WF-A2 shows everything about one owner: listings, funnel, revenue, cost, surveys, errors, behaviour signals, and recommendations. Needs role-based access, PII masking, multi-endpoint aggregation, and real-time error logs. Key output is profit per owner, onboarding status, and churn risk. This is the owner-level CRM + business intelligence panel.”
        
        ---
        
    - **WF-A3 — Integrations & Error Logs (Admin + Founder)**
        
        ---
        
        **Audience:** Founder + Admin (NOT visible to Support / NOT to Developers unless granted).
        
        **Purpose:** Central place to check system health, portal syncs, API connections, and error logs.
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣ Designer Checklist**
        
        - Use Dashfolio+ dark theme
        - Group integrations as **cards** (Rightmove, Zoopla, WhatsApp, Calendar, Stripe, Email, AI Engine, Survey Engine, Hosting)
        - Each card shows:
            - Green/Yellow/Red status light
            - Last sync timestamp
            - Errors count (last 24h)
            - Button: “View Logs”
            - Button: “Retry Sync”
        - Error Logs displayed in collapsible table with:
            - Timestamp
            - Integration
            - Severity (Critical / Warning / Info)
            - Affected listing or user
            - Error message (shortened)
            - “View Details”
        - Sticky top header with:
            - “System Integrations”
            - Global Health Indicator
        - Add “System Recommendations” block at bottom
        - Keep typography consistent with Owner/Admin WF
        
        ---
        
        # **2️⃣ Developer Checklist**
        
        **Endpoints required:**
        
        ```
        /admin/integrations/health
        /admin/integrations/:service/logs
        /admin/integrations/:service/retry
        /admin/system/errors
        /admin/system/warnings
        ```
        
        **Logging requirements:**
        
        - Every integration call must log:
            - request payload (for Founder only)
            - response code
            - latency
            - error message
            - related user/listing ID
        
        **Audit trail:**
        
        - Log whenever Admin or Founder:
            - views sensitive logs
            - clicks “Retry Sync”
            - clicks “View API Response”
            - updates API key (Founder only)
        
        **Security:**
        
        - API keys masked: sk_live_****39FJ
        - Non-Founders cannot see full keys
        - Support cannot access this page at all
        - Error messages sanitized to avoid exposing secure tokens
        
        ---
        
        # **3️⃣ Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
        
        Not customer-facing.
        
        WF-A3 is where Admin checks WHY a listing isn’t updating or why an owner is experiencing problems.
        
        Examples:
        
        - Rightmove feed failed → owner sees no views
        - WhatsApp delivery failed → owner thinks buyer ignored them
        - Calendar sync broken → buyers can’t book
        - Stripe error → subscription not active
        
        WF-A3 gives Admin **diagnosis + repair tools**.
        
        ---
        
        # **4️⃣ User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
        
        This page appears when Admin clicks:
        
        - “Integrations” from Admin Dashboard
        - “System error” from any page
        - “Retry” link from WF-A2 Owner Detail
        - “Sync Logs” footer
        
        WF-A3 is a **technical command center**, not for everyday use unless errors occur.
        
        ---
        
        # **5️⃣ Purpose**
        
        WF-A3 exists to answer:
        
        ### **“What is broken, why is it broken, and what do we do about it?”**
        
        It provides:
        
        - System status
        - Integration uptime
        - Error logs
        - Retry actions
        - Error → user impact mapping
        - Recommendations
        
        This is your **DevOps & Monitoring** panel without needing DevOps.
        
        ---
        
        # **6️⃣ What This Page Should Solve**
        
        ✔ Identify problems FAST
        
        ✔ Show which users are impacted
        
        ✔ Show which listings are not syncing
        
        ✔ Help Admin fix simple issues (“Retry Sync”)
        
        ✔ Allow Founder to update API keys
        
        ✔ Provide root cause analysis
        
        ✔ Alert Founder about patterns (e.g. Twilio bill spike)
        
        ✔ Show downtime
        
        ✔ Show recommendation on next actions
        
        ---
        
        # **7️⃣ What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
        
        ### **7.1 Top Section: System Health Grid**
        
        Large cards with status:
        
        | **Integration** | **Status** | **Last Sync** | **Errors 24h** | **Actions** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        | Rightmove | 🟢 OK | 2 mins ago | 0 | View Logs / Retry |
        | Zoopla | 🟡 Warning | 19 mins ago | 4 | View Logs / Retry |
        | OTM | 🟢 OK | 4 mins ago | 0 | View Logs / Retry |
        | WhatsApp | 🔴 Critical | 1h ago | 21 | View Logs / Retry |
        | Stripe | 🟢 OK | 3 mins ago | 0 | Billing Dashboard |
        | Calendar | 🟡 Slow | 12 mins ago | 2 | View Logs / Retry |
        | Email | 🟢 OK | 1 min ago | 0 | View Logs |
        | AI Engine | 🟡 Latency High | 8 mins ago | 3 | View Logs |
        | Map API | 🟢 | Real-time | 0 | Usage Stats |
        | Hosting | 🟢 | Uptime 99.99% | 0 | Server Logs |
        
        ---
        
        ### **7.2 Error Logs Table**
        
        Columns:
        
        - Timestamp
        - Severity (red/yellow/blue)
        - Integration
        - Affected: Owner / Buyer / Listing ID
        - Error Summary
        - “View Details” (modal)
        - “Retry Sync” (if applicable)
        
        ---
        
        ### **7.3 Error Details Modal**
        
        Shows:
        
        - Full error
        - Request
        - Response
        - Impact analysis
        - Suggested fix
        - “Apply Fix” (Founder only)
        
        ---
        
        ### **7.4 System Recommendations Panel**
        
        AI auto-suggests solutions:
        
        - “WhatsApp API error rate increased 42% — check Twilio balance.”
        - “Rightmove API latency spike — consider upgrading plan.”
        - “High error rate for one listing — address issue with owner.”
        - “Recurring error: wrong postcode format → auto-sanitize.”
        
        ---
        
        # **8️⃣ Developer Requirements (deep)**
        
        ### **8.1 Services monitored:**
        
        - Rightmove JSON feed
        - Zoopla JSON feed
        - OnTheMarket feed
        - WhatsApp API
        - Email SMTP
        - Calendar ICS
        - Stripe API
        - AI API
        - Hosting uptime
        - Map API
        
        ### **8.2 Error Classification**
        
        ```
        Critical → integration down
        Warning → degraded performance
        Info → retry succeeded
        Notice → expected behaviour
        ```
        
        ### **8.3 Log retention**
        
        - Store 14 days for admin
        - 90 days for Founder
        - Mask sensitive fields
        - Export CSV (Founder only)
        
        ---
        
        # **9️⃣ KPI Definitions (Integration KPIs)**
        
        | **KPI** | **Meaning** |
        | --- | --- |
        | Sync Success Rate | % of successful portal updates |
        | Error Rate (24h) | number of exceptions |
        | Latency | average ms per integration call |
        | Delivery Ratio (WhatsApp) | delivered / sent messages |
        | Calendar Acceptance Rate | buyer→owner sync reliability |
        | Stripe Failure Rate | failed payments |
        | Hosting Uptime | monitored via ping service |
        
        ---
        
        # **🔟 Conversion Funnel (Technical Reliability)**
        
        Not user-facing.
        
        ```
        Attempted Sync → Successful Sync → Delivered to Portal → Portal Confirmed
        ```
        
        If any fails → error triggers WF-A3.
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣1️⃣ Integration Logic (technical model)**
        
        Each integration stores:
        
        ```
        integrationName
        lastSync
        lastStatus
        lastError
        affectedListings[]
        affectedUsers[]
        errorFrequency
        latency
        retryCount
        apiKeyValid (boolean)
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣2️⃣ Developer Tooling Overview**
        
        WF-A3 interacts with:
        
        - Logging service
        - Portal APIs
        - Twilio API
        - Stripe telemetry
        - Hosting monitoring
        - AI error classifier
        - Internal “Retry Engine”
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣3️⃣ Dummy Content (for Designer)**
        
        **Example Logs Table Row**
        
        ```
        [12:41:08]
        CRITICAL
        WhatsApp API
        Owner #1183 (12 King Street)
        "Twilio: rate limit exceeded"
        Retry Sync
        ```
        
        **Example Recommendations**
        
        > “Twilio balance critically low (£0.86 remaining). Top up recommended.”
        > 
        
        > “Zoopla feed returned 502 — retry scheduled automatically.”
        > 
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣4️⃣ Rental Logic (Integrated)**
        
        Integrations do NOT change between sale/rent.
        
        Only difference:
        
        - Rental EPC is mandatory — flagged in error logs.
        - Calendar may need additional fields (tenant info required).
        - Portal feed must map rental-specific fields:
            - rent-per-month
            - deposit
            - furnishing
        
        WF-A3 shows errors if these fields are missing.
        
        ---
        
        # **⚡️ 30-Second Dev Summary**
        
        “WF-A3 shows health of all platform integrations. Includes sync status, error logs, retry actions, and system recommendations. Requires secure endpoints, PII masking, error classification, audit logging, and integration with portal APIs, Twilio, Stripe, and hosting telemetry. This is the Admin technical monitoring page.”
        
        ---
        
    - **WF-A4 — Tasks & Fulfillment (Admin + Support + Founder)**
        
        This page is ESSENTIAL for running NoAgent operationally:
        
        - every sign to dispatch
        - every EPC to order
        - every photo to schedule
        - every verification to check
        - every issue to fix
        - every support escalation
        - every owner onboarding block
        - every “system recommendation” that becomes a task
        
        Everything is captured here.
        
        ---
        
        # **Audience:** Founder, Admin, Support (with role-based restrictions)
        
        **Purpose:** Centralised operational To-Do system for all actions across Owners, Buyers, Listings, Integrations.
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣ Designer Checklist**
        
        - Dark Dashfolio+ style
        - Use a **3-lane Kanban board**
            - **To Do**
            - **In Progress**
            - **Done**
        - Ability to switch to **Table view**
        - Add a **“Create Task” button** (top-right)
        - Each task card must show:
            - title
            - task type (colour-coded)
            - owner/listing reference
            - due date
            - assigned staff
            - priority (Low/Med/High/Critical)
        - Filters on top:
            - Task Type
            - Status
            - Assigned To
            - Priority
            - Auto-created vs Manual
        - Add collapsible side panel:
            - Task details
            - Notes
            - Activity log
            - Linked objects (listing, owner, buyer, error)
        - Include a “Bulk Actions” dropdown:
            - assign
            - change priority
            - mark done
        - Visual indicators for:
            - overdue tasks
            - urgent tasks
            - blocked tasks
        - Keep spacing large, readable, functional
        
        ---
        
        # **2️⃣ Developer Checklist**
        
        **Endpoints required:**
        
        ```
        /admin/tasks
        /admin/tasks/create
        /admin/tasks/:id
        /admin/tasks/assign
        /admin/tasks/complete
        /admin/tasks/bulk
        ```
        
        **Task Object Model:**
        
        ```
        taskID
        title
        description
        taskType
        priority
        status
        createdBy
        assignedTo
        relatedOwnerID
        relatedListingID
        relatedBuyerID
        relatedIntegration
        dueDate
        createdAt
        updatedAt
        auditTrail[]
        autoGenerated (boolean)
        ```
        
        **Audit Trail must log:**
        
        - creation
        - assignment
        - field changes
        - completion
        - unmask actions
        - comments
        
        **Role permissions:**
        
        | **Field** | **Founder** | **Admin** | **Support** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        | Create task | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ |
        | Assign task | ✓ | ✓ | ✗ |
        | Change priority | ✓ | ✓ | ✗ |
        | Delete task | ✓ | ✗ | ✗ |
        | View PII | ✓ | ✓ (masked) | masked |
        | Mark completed | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ |
        
        **Performance:**
        
        - Cache tasks for speed
        - Real-time update (websocket optional)
        
        ---
        
        # **3️⃣ Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
        
        WF-A4 helps Admin support Owners:
        
        - when an owner is stuck in onboarding
        - when listings aren’t syncing
        - when EPC or floorplans are missing
        - when viewings must be scheduled
        - when a sign must be delivered
        - when support tickets escalate
        - when owner is unresponsive
        - when offers need manual confirmation
        - when surveys must be checked
        
        Essentially: this page keeps Owners moving.
        
        ---
        
        # **4️⃣ User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
        
        WF-A4 opens when Admin clicks:
        
        - “Tasks” from Admin Dashboard
        - “Create Task” from:
            - Owner Detail (WF-A2)
            - Buyer Detail (WF-A5)
            - Integration Errors (WF-A3)
            - Survey marketplace
            - Support message
        
        This page replaces Slack/Notion for internal operations.
        
        ---
        
        # **5️⃣ Purpose**
        
        WF-A4 ensures NoAgent operations run smoothly:
        
        **✔ Fulfillment of services**

        ✔ EPC bookings
        
        ✔ Sign delivery

        The Admin system must prevent chaos.

        ✔ Central place for all Admin / Support work
        
        ✔ Track service delivery
        
        ✔ Track onboarding issues
        
        ✔ Ensure nothing is forgotten
        
        ✔ Automatically generate tasks from errors

        | --- | --- | --- |

        - Title
        - Full description
        - Priority dropdown
        - Status dropdown
        - Assigned to dropdown
        - Related Owner / Listing / Buyer
        - Subtasks (optional)
        - Activity log
        - “Mark Done” button
        
        ---
        
        ### **7.5 Auto-Generated Tasks (AI)**
        
        Examples:
        
        - “Rightmove sync failed for Listing #222”
        - “Owner not replied to 3 buyers in 48 hours”
        - “Photos missing for high-performing listing — recommend scheduling shoot”
        - “Survey uploaded — check compliance and set price”
        
        These appear with **‘Auto’ tag**.
        
        ---
        
        # **8️⃣ Developer Requirements (Deep)**
        
        ### **Task Generation Logic**
        
        Auto-create tasks for:
        
        ### **1. Owner Issues**
        
        - onboarding stuck
        - missing price
        - missing photos
        - missing EPC
        - no viewing slots
        
        ### **2. Buyer Issues**
        
        - verification pending
        - fraudulent patterns
        - incomplete offer
        
        ### **3. Integration Issues**
        
        - Twilio failure
        - Portal sync failure
        - Calendar sync failure
        
        ### **4. System Recommendations**
        
        - price change suggestions
        - photo needs
        - survey resale opportunity
        
        ---
        
        ### **Notifications**
        
        - Email (Admin)
        - WhatsApp (optional)
        - Admin page highlight
        
        ---
        
        ### **Task SLA**
        
        Developer must implement deadlines:
        
        - Critical: 24 hours
        - High: 48 hours
        - Medium: 4 days
        - Low: 7 days
        
        ---
        
        # **9️⃣ KPI Definitions**
        
        | **KPI** | **Meaning** |
        | --- | --- |
        | Open Tasks | total tasks not completed |
        | SLA Breach | overdue tasks |
        | Service Completion Rate | photos/EPC delivered |
        | Avg Task Age | days open |
        | Auto-generated Tasks | system issues count |
        | Manual Tasks | human-created |
        | Staff Load | tasks per staff |

        ```
        Issue Detected → Task Created (auto/manual) → Assigned → Action Taken → Resolved
        ```
        
        WF-A4 visualises every stage.

        ---
        
        # **WF-A5 — Buyer Detail View (Admin)**
        
        **Audience:** Founder, Admin, Support
        
        **Purpose:** A complete 360° view of every Home-Hunter (buyer/tenant).
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣ Designer Checklist**
        
        - Keep Dashfolio+ dark theme
        - Layout similar to WF-A2 (Owner Detail) for consistency
        - Left column: Buyer profile summary
        - Main area: Tabs
            - Overview
            - Offers
            - Viewings
            - Messages
            - Documents & Verification
            - Activity Log
        - Each tab uses Framer components (cards, tables, badges)
        - Add badges:
            - Verified / Unverified
            - Cash / Mortgage / Just Browsing
            - New / Returning
        - Mandatory visual elements:
            - Buyer avatar placeholder
            - Phone + email masked (role-dependent)
            - Timeline of actions
        - Add “Create Task” button
        - Add “Flag Buyer” button
        - Keep spacing large and readable

        ```

        /admin/buyer/:id/viewings
        /admin/buyer/:id/messages
        /admin/buyer/:id/verify
        /admin/buyer/:id/documents
        ```
        
        **Backend requirements:**
        
        - Buyer ID linking to **Offers, Viewings, Inquiries, Surveys, Verifications**
        - Permission matrix for PII masking
        - Verification workflow:
            - Upload ID
            - Upload Proof of Funds / Mortgage in Principle
            - Admin approval
        - Risk scoring engine
        - Activity logging
        - Buyer state transitions:
            - New → Active → Verified → High Intent → Offer Made → Under Negotiation
        
        • P**rofit per Owner / Buyer activity** comes from WF-A8 + analytics.
        
        ---
        
        # **3️⃣ Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
        
        Owners rely on the Admin to:
        
        - validate buyers
        - confirm serious offers
        - escalate suspicious inquiries
        - organise viewing schedules
        - evaluate buyer documents
        - send qualified offers only
        
        WF-A5 helps Admin protect the Owner experience.

        - WF-H pages (Admin override)
        
        This is the main **investigation / verification / decision page**.

        - assign tasks to support
        - flag problematic accounts
        - ensure secure + fair offers for Owners

        | 9 Rose Lane | £399,000 | Jan 9 | Withdrawn | — |

        - Completed viewings
        - No-shows
        - Reschedules
        - Group viewings vs private
        
        ---
        
        **Tab 4 — Messages**
        
        Shows messaging thread between buyer ↔ owner (masked phone).
        
        Admin can step in:
        
        - join conversation
        - leave notes
        - send templated replies
        
        ---
        
        **Tab 5 — Documents & Verification**
        
        Card layout:
        
        - ID (uploaded)
        - Proof of Address
        - Proof of Funds
        - Mortgage in Principle
        - KYC Score
        - Verification Status
        - “Approve / Reject / Request More Info”
        
        ---
        
        **Tab 6 — Activity Log**
        
        Full chronological log:
        
        ```
        Jan 10 — Buyer made offer on 12 King St.
        Jan 8  — Buyer attended viewing.
        Jan 6  — Buyer uploaded Mortgage in Principle.
        Jan 6  — Buyer created account.
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **8️⃣ Developer Requirements**
        
        ### **PII Display Logic**
        
        - Founder: full unmasked
        - Admin: masked email/phone except verification stage
        - Support: always masked
        
        ### **Offer Scoring Logic**
        
        Factors:
        
        - offer amount vs asking
        - buyer funding type
        - document completeness
        - viewing attendance
        - risk flags
        
        ### **Risk Engine**
        
        Flags:
        
        - inconsistent info
        - duplicate accounts
        - mismatched documents
        - failed AML checks
        - unusually high/low offers
        
        ### **Verification Workflow**
        
        - document upload → OCR check → admin review
        - store verification events in auditTrail
        
        ### **Activity Capture**
        
        Every interaction stored:
        
        ```
        viewingBooked
        messageSent
        offerMade
        documentUploaded
        verificationStatusChanged
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **9️⃣ KPI Definitions**
        
        | **KPI** | **Meaning** |
        | --- | --- |
        | Verification Score | % of documents approved |
        | Offer Strength | Weighted score |
        | Viewing Conversion | Viewings → Offers |
        | Engagement Score | Inquiries + messages |
        | Risk Score | Fraud likelihood |
        | Survey Use | Buyer purchased shared surveys |

        → Viewing Booked

    - **WF-A6 — Survey Marketplace Oversight**
        
        This is one of the most strategically important admin screens — because surveys can become a **high-margin revenue engine** for NoAgent.
        
        ---
        
        **Audience:** Founder / Admin Only**
        
        **Purpose:** Manage all surveys uploaded, shared, purchased, validated, and connected to listings.
        
        This is the “Surveys Command Center”.
        
        ---
        
        # **1️⃣ Designer Checklist**
        
        - Use Dashfolio+ dark theme
        - Keep same structural layout as WF-A2 & WF-A5 for consistency
        - Left sidebar filter:
            - Status (Available / Requested / Pending Owner Approval / Sold / Expired)
            - Place (dropdown)
            - Surveyor (dropdown)
        - Main view = **tables + detail drawers**
        - Survey cards must show:
            - Price
            - Report type
            - Validity
            - Buyer count
        - Detail drawer (side panel) includes:
            - Full survey info
            - Associated Place
            - Download buttons
            - Flags, notes, tasks
        - Buttons needed:
            - “Upload New Survey”
            - “Approve Survey”
            - “Request Correction”
            - “Set Price”
            - “Share with Buyers”
        - Use colored status badges
        - Keep spacing consistent with WF-A5
        
        ---
        
        # **2️⃣ Developer Checklist**
        
        - Endpoints:
        
        ```
        /admin/surveys
        /admin/surveys/:surveyID
        /admin/surveys/create
        /admin/surveys/:surveyID/approve
        /admin/surveys/:surveyID/setPrice
        /admin/surveys/:surveyID/share
        ```
        
        - Survey storage (likely S3 bucket)
        - OCR extraction (optional future phase)
        - Link surveys to:
            - Listings
            - Owners
            - Buyers
            - Offers
        - Track survey “version history”
        - Log all actions in auditTrail
        - Permission system:
            - Only Founder can delete surveys
            - Admin can approve/reject
            - Support can request missing info
        - Revenue tracking:
            - Commission per re-sale
            - Marketplace sales count
            - Payout to surveyor (if external)
        
        ---
        
        # **3️⃣ Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
        
        Owners may:
        
        - upload their own survey
        - buy discounted surveys
        - allow other buyers to access
        - reduce time to sale
        - streamline decision making
        
        WF-A6 ensures the marketplace is **clean, verified, accurate**.
        
        ---
        
        # **4️⃣ User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
        
        Admin reaches WF-A6 via:
        
        - WF-A2 (Owner Detail View → “Surveys” section)
        - WF-A5 (Buyer Detail View → “Purchased Surveys”)
        - Global Admin Sidebar → “Surveys Marketplace Oversight”
        - WF-O5 (Public Page → “Survey Available” → Admin approval)
        
        ---
        
        # **5️⃣ Purpose**
        
        WF-A6 is designed to:
        
        - centralise all survey files
        - ensure surveys meet quality & compliance
        - manage pricing strategy
        - detect fraudulent or duplicate surveys
        - track buyer engagement
        - maximise re-sale value (your revenue)
        - give fast insight into survey popularity & ROI
        
        ---
        
        # **6️⃣ What This Page Should Solve**
        
        ✔ Stop bad/fake surveys
        
        ✔ Let Admin price surveys smartly (dynamic pricing)
        
        ✔ Make surveys instantly available to buyers
        
        ✔ Track revenue from survey resale
        
        ✔ Act as arbitrage engine: buy once → sell multiple times
        
        ✔ Provide transparent history
        
        ✔ Enable corrections & version updates
        
        ✔ Give Admin full control of which survey is active

            - Billing

        # **8️⃣ Developer Requirements**
        
        ### **Ticket Creation Logic**
        
        Tickets created:
        
        1. User manually reports → support ticket created
        2. System integration error → auto ticket
        3. Owner issues from WF-O2/WF-O3/WF-O4 → ticket with context
        4. Buyer issues from WF-H flows → ticket with context
        5. Billing failure → auto ticket + Stripe event
        
        ### **SLA Rules**
        
        - High priority: 2h
        - Medium: 6h
        - Low: 24h
        
        Timer visible in UI.
        
        ### **Role-Based Masking**
        
        - Support sees masked PII
        - Admin sees full contact
        - Founder sees everything including risk logs
        
        ### **Notification Triggers**
        
        - New ticket
        - SLA approaching
        - Owner responds
        - Buyer responds

        | --- | --- |
        | First Response Time | Avg time to first reply |
        | Resolution Time | Avg time to close |
        | Auto-Resolved Rate | % solved without human |
        | Ticket Escalation Rate | % escalated to-Founder |
        | Recurring Issue Count | Tickets with repeated cause |
        | Integration Error Rate | Failures creating auto-tickets |
        | User Satisfaction | Rating after ticket closure |

    - **WF-A8 — Billing & Subscription Overview**
        
        We will build **Hybrid-Ready, MVP-Active Billing**, meaning:

        - Survey payouts
        - Multi-country VAT
        - Marketplace revenue splits
        
        This gives you:
        
        ✔ no migration later
        
        ✔ scalable foundation
        
        ✔ predictable income

        ✔ flexibility for Germany
        
        ✔ future-proof architecture

        # **8️⃣ Developer Requirements**
        
        ### **Revenue Calculation**

        ### **Cost Calculation**

        ### **Profit Calculation**
