    - **WF-A9 — Admin Analytics & Performance Dashboard** (optional)
        
        ---
        
        **Audience:** Founder + Admin (NOT Support)
        
        **Purpose:** Strategic analytics over weeks/months, not day-to-day operations. Think *“Are we growing? What’s working? Where should we invest?”*
        
        ---
        
        ## **1️⃣ Designer Checklist**
        
        - Dark Dashfolio+ theme, consistent typography.
        - This is **NOT** a cluttered metrics page. Think:
            - Big clear charts
            - 2–3 metrics per section
            - Time filters (7 / 30 / 90 days; custom range)
        - Layout:
            - Row 1: High-level “North Star” metrics.
            - Row 2: Funnels and behaviour charts.
            - Row 3: Revenue and profitability charts.
            - Row 4: Experiments / country comparison (later).
        - All numbers readable on desktop first; mobile: stack sections vertically.
        - Use the same colour logic everywhere:
            - Green = good / growth
            - Yellow = neutral / watch
            - Red = problem
        - Hover tooltips on charts for exact values.
        - Keep this visually distinct from WF-A1 (less “alerts”, more “insight”).
        
        ---
        
        ## **2️⃣ Developer Checklist**
        
        **You will need aggregation endpoints, not raw row-level stuff:**
        
        - /admin/analytics/summary
        - /admin/analytics/funnels
        - /admin/analytics/owners
        - /admin/analytics/buyers
        - /admin/analytics/countries
        - /admin/analytics/revenue
        
        Key requirements:
        
        - All heavy calculations done **server-side**, not in the browser.
        - Time-window filters (start_date, end_date).
        - Grouping by:
            - day / week / month
            - country (UK, Germany, later others)
            - plan (Basic / Enhanced / Pro)
        - Must be **read-only**; no editing from this page.
        - Respect role: Founder can see profit and cost; Admin may see only revenue and operational metrics (configurable).
        
        ---
        
        ## **3️⃣ Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
        
        WF-A9 looks at the **overall journey**, not one person:
        
        > How do Owners move through:
        > 
        
        > Sign up → Create place → Publish → Viewings → Offers → Sold / Rented
        > 
        
        And:
        
        > Are we getting more of them, faster, and more profitably?
        > 
        
        ---
        
        ## **4️⃣ User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
        
        You land on A9 when:
        
        - Founder clicks “Analytics” from WF-A1 (Admin Dashboard).
        - Admin wants to answer “How did we perform this month?”.
        - You’re preparing investor-style or internal “monthly review”.
        
        This is **strategic**, not a daily “fix stuff” screen.
        
        ---
        
        ## **5️⃣ Purpose**
        
        WF-A9 should answer questions like:
        
        - Are we growing Owners and Home-Hunters month on month?
        - Are our funnels improving or getting worse?
        - Which packages and services actually make money?
        - Is survey marketplace working?
        - Is Germany worth it vs UK?
        - Where should we invest: SEO, surveys, services, pricing changes?
        
        ---
        
        ## **6️⃣ What This Page Should Solve**
        
        ✔ Show growth trends (not just snapshots).
        
        ✔ Visualise funnels over time (conversion improving or not).
        
        ✔ Compare performance by channel (Rightmove vs direct vs sign).
        
        ✔ Compare UK vs Germany performance.
        
        ✔ Break down revenue by source (subscriptions, add-ons, surveys).
        
        ✔ Track churn and retention patterns.
        
        ✔ Provide insight into which levers work (viewings, pricing changes, services).
        
        ---
        
        ## **7️⃣ What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
        
        ### **7.1 Row 1 — “North Star” Overview**
        
        Four big cards with sparkline charts underneath:
        
        - **Active Owners (30 days)**
        - **New Owners (30 days)**
        - **Active Home-Hunters (30 days)**
        - **Total Places Sold / Rented (30 days)**
        
        Each card shows:
        
        - current value
        - change vs previous period (+12% / –7%)
        
        ---
        
        ### **7.2 Row 2 — Conversion Funnels (Global)**
        
        Two charts side by side:
        
        **Chart A — Owner Funnel (stacked bar or flow)**
        
        Stages (percentage and count):
        
        - Owners signed up
        - Owners created first place
        - Owners published
        - Owners with first viewing
        - Owners with at least one offer
        - Owners with sold/rented outcome
        
        **Chart B — Buyer Funnel**
        
        Stages:
        
        - Home-Hunters registered
        - Booked viewing
        - Verified documents
        - Made offer
        - Offer accepted
        
        Each funnel has filters for time range and country.
        
        ---
        
        ### **7.3 Row 3 — Revenue & Profitability Trends**
        
        **Left:** Line chart
        
        - “Total Revenue per month”
        - Option to split by:
            - subscriptions
            - add-ons
            - surveys
        
        **Right:** Line or bar chart
        
        - “Net Profit per month” (only for Founder)
            - with a thin secondary line for “Total Costs”
        
        Below: small bar chart
        
        - “Revenue by plan” (Basic / Enhanced / Pro).
        
        ---
        
        ### **7.4 Row 4 — Channels & Country Comparison**
        
        **Channels Performance Chart (stacked bar or pie)**
        
        - Rightmove
        - Zoopla
        - OnTheMarket
        - Yalla.House direct (website)
        - Sign with QR code
        - Social media / ads
        
        Metrics per channel:
        
        - views
        - inquiries
        - viewings
        - offers
        - deals done
        
        **Country Comparison Card**
        
        - UK vs Germany (once live)
            
            Show:
            
        - average revenue per owner
        - average time to sell
        - average cost per listing
        - margin per country
        
        ---
        
        ### **7.5 Row 5 — Survey Marketplace Analytics**
        
        Small section (important for future):
        
        - surveys uploaded per month
        - surveys purchased per month
        - average resale count per survey (reuse)
        - survey revenue and profit
        
        ---
        
        ### **7.6 Row 6 — “Insights & Recommendations”**
        
        A card list like:
        
        - “Owner conversion from sign-up → publish decreased by 11% this month. Consider improving onboarding tips.”
        - “Survey sales grew 22%. Maybe highlight this service more on public pages.”
        - “Rightmove channel brings 60% of views but 45% of deals. Signs bring 10% of views but 20% of deals (high intent).”
        
        ---
        
        ## **8️⃣ Developer Requirements**
        
        ### **Aggregations needed**
        
        - Daily/weekly/monthly counts of:
            - new owners
            - new home-hunters
            - active listings
            - viewings
            - offers
            - deals
        - Funnels:
            - counts per stage (stored or computed via events)
        - Revenue:
            - group by month, by source, by plan
        - Cost:
            - aggregated from Airtable / internal cost table
        - Survey stats:
            - number of uploads
            - number of purchases
            - revenue and cost
        
        ### **Performance**
        
        - Pre-aggregate in a nightly job where possible.
        - Only recompute “today so far” live.
        - Avoid reading millions of raw rows for every page load.
        
        ---
        
        ## **9️⃣ KPI Definitions (Strategic)**
        
        To keep it human-readable, no raw acronyms without explanation:
        
        - **Monthly Recurring Revenue**
            
            Recurring subscription revenue per month.
            
        - **Average Revenue per Owner**
            
            Total revenue divided by number of paying Owners.
            
        - **Owner Retention**
            
            Owners who remain active (keep at least one active place) after 3 / 6 / 12 months.
            
        - **Churn Rate**
            
            Owners who cancel / go inactive per month.
            
        - **Time to First Viewing**
            
            Average days from “place published” to first viewing booked.
            
        - **Time to Sold / Rented**
            
            Average days from “place published” to “deal done”.
            
        - **Survey Reuse Rate**
            
            Average number of buyers using one survey.
            
        - **Channel Efficiency**
            
            Deals per 100 viewings per channel.
            
        
        ---
        
        ## **🔟 Conversion Funnels (At Analytics Level)**
        
        ### **Owner funnel**
        
        Sign up → Start listing → Publish → First viewing → Offer → Deal
        
        ### **Buyer funnel**
        
        Sign up → Book viewing → Verify → Offer → Offer accepted
        
        Both visualised and measured over time.
        
        ---
        
        ## **1️⃣1️⃣ Analytics Data Model (High Level)**
        
        You do **not** need to expose this in the UI, but useful for dev:
        
        ```
        analytics_events
          - eventID
          - userID
          - role (owner / buyer)
          - type (signup, create_place, publish, viewing_booked, offer_made, survey_purchased, etc.)
          - placeID
          - country
          - timestamp
          - channel (RM/ZP/OTM/sign/direct/etc.)
        
        analytics_daily_summary
          - date
          - country
          - owners_new
          - owners_active
          - buyers_new
          - places_published
          - viewings
          - offers
          - deals
          - revenue_subscriptions
          - revenue_addons
          - revenue_surveys
          - costs_total
        ```
        
        ---
        
        ## **1️⃣2️⃣ Developer Tooling Overview**
        
        WF-A9 pulls from:
        
        - analytics_events (or similar)
        - daily/monthly summary tables
        - Stripe (for revenue)
        - Airtable or internal table (for costs)
        - survey stats
        - channel mapping (origin of traffic/viewings)
        
        No write actions here, **read-only analytics**.
        
        ---
        
        ## **1️⃣3️⃣ Dummy Content (for Designer)**
        
        Example copy you can drop in:
        
        > Last 30 days — Snapshot
        > 
        
        > • 18 new Owners (+22%)
        > 
        
        > • 47 new Home-Hunters (+15%)
        > 
        
        > • 12 places sold / rented
        > 
        
        > • Time to sold: 39 days (median)
        > 
        
        > Owner funnel (last 30 days)
        > 
        
        > • 100 sign-ups → 70 started a listing → 52 published → 31 had viewings → 11 had offers → 8 sold/rented
        > 
        
        > Channel highlights
        > 
        
        > • Rightmove: 54% of views, 47% of deals
        > 
        
        > • QR sign: 9% of views, 19% of deals (high intent)
        > 
        
        ---
        
        ## **1️⃣4️⃣ Rental Logic (Included by Design)**
        
        All charts must be filterable by:
        
        - **Sale vs Rent vs Both**
        
        So you can see e.g.:
        
        - “Time to rent” vs “Time to sell”
        - “Average rent per place” trends
        - “Rent vs Sell conversion per channel”
        
        The data model is the same; just filter on listing type.
        
        ---
        
        ## **⚡ 30-Second Developer Summary**
        
        “WF-A9 is a read-only strategic analytics page: trends, funnels, revenue vs cost, channels, and country performance. It uses aggregated tables, not raw events. Must support time filters and breakdown by country and channel. No writes, no PII – just business intelligence.”

    - **🧩 WF-A2 — Owner Detail View (Admin 360° Overview)**
        
        *(MVP + Phase 2. Expansion-ready. Single source of truth.)*
        
        ```
        ──────────────────────────────
               WF-A2 — OWNER DETAIL
        ──────────────────────────────
        ```
        
        # **1. Designer Checklist**
        
        - Use **card layout** (Dashfolio+ default)
        - Keep everything modular (stacked sections)
        - Use **2-column layout** on desktop, fully stacked on mobile
        - Use **Yalla Yellow** ONLY for status tags & action buttons
        - Owner name & avatar as page header (like a CRM profile)
        - Clear separation between:
            - Owner info
            - Listings
            - Activity timeline
            - Tasks
            - Billing & subscriptions
            - Survey uploads
            - Communication logs
        
        ---
        
        # **2. Developer Checklist**
        
        - One endpoint:
            
            **GET /admin/owner/{ownerID}**
            
            Must return aggregated data:
            
            - Owner profile
            - Listings (draft, live, under offer, sold/let)
            - Billing history
            - Support tickets
            - Tasks linked to owner
            - Activity log
            - Surveys uploaded
            - Tracking tags
            - Country + language
            - Login activity
        - Build reusable subcomponents:
            - ListingsTable
            - BillingTable
            - ActivityFeed
            - TasksPanel
            - SupportConversationPreview
        - Phase 2: Caching + event-based updates.
        
        ---
        
        # **3. Admin Journey (Short Summary)**
        
        Admin lands here by:
        
        - Clicking an Owner in **A2 — Owners List**
        - Clicking from Tickets (A5)
        - Clicking from Tasks (A6)
        - Clicking from Billing events (A8)
        
        This is the **main CRM page** for every seller/landlord.
        
        ---
        
        # **4. User Journey (Context)**
        
        ```
        A1 Dashboard
           ↓ click Owner
        A2 Owner Detail View
           ↓
        Listings (O2)
        Invoices (A8)
        Support (A5)
        Tasks (A6)
        Integrations (A4)
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **5. Purpose**
        
        This page must give the Admin (or support staff) an **instant understanding** of:
        
        - Who the owner is
        - What they are selling
        - How far along they are
        - What tasks are pending
        - What revenue is expected
        - What issues have occurred
        - How engaged they are
        
        ---
        
        # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
        
        - Identify owners who need support
        - Track listing progress
        - Resolve errors quickly
        - View financial contributions
        - Understand conversion/performance
        - Manage workflows (photo orders, EPC, sign delivery)
        - See all communication in one place
        
        ---
        
        # **7. What the Designer Should Build (Framer Layout)**
        
        ## **A. Owner Header Card**
        
        ## **(Top of page)**
        
        - Owner Name
        - Email
        - Phone
        - Country flag (auto-detected from phone/IP)
        - Joined date
        - Last login
        - Status tags:
            - Active
            - Inactive
            - Requires Support
        - Quick Actions:
            - **Message Owner** (opens internal admin → owner thread)
            - **Create Task**
            - **View Billing**
        
        ---
        
        ## **B. Listings Overview Section**
        
        ## **(MVP)**
        
        Table:
        
        | **Thumbnail** | **Address** | **Type** | **Status** | **Views** | **Inquiries** | **Actions** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        
        Actions → “Open Listing (as Admin)” → Links to O2.
        
        **Phase 2:**
        
        - Heatmaps
        - Listing health score
        - Recommended actions
        
        ---
        
        ## **C. Activity Timeline**
        
        Chronological feed:
        
        - Listing created
        - Price change
        - New inquiry received
        - Viewing booked
        - Offer submitted
        - Survey uploaded
        - Support ticket opened/closed
        - Tasks created/finished
        
        ---
        
        ## **D. Tasks Related to This Owner**
        
        Mini Kanban:
        
        - To Do
            - EPC required
            - Rightmove push pending
        - In Progress
            - Signboard printing
        - Done
            - Photographers booked
        
        Clicking opens A6.
        
        ---
        
        ## **E. Support History**
        
        - List of all tickets by this owner
        - Ticket status
        - Last message
        - Response time metrics
            
            Click → A5 Support Inbox (filtered view).
            
        
        ---
        
        ## **F. Billing & Subscription**
        
        - Package: Free / Basic / Premium
        - Next billing date
        - Invoices (from Stripe)
        - Total revenue generated
        - Refunds / disputes
        - Payment issues (flagged)
        
        ---
        
        ## **G. Surveys (If owner uploaded)**
        
        - Uploaded surveys
        - Verification status
        - Earnings (if applicable — future feature)
        
        ---
        
        # **8. Developer Requirements**
        
        ### **MVP:**
        
        - Simple REST endpoint
        - SQL joins: owners + listings + tasks + tickets + billing
        - No heavy analytics
        - Fetch real-time Stripe events
        - Activity feed generated from unified event table (system_events)
        - Caching optional
        
        ### **Phase 2:**
        
        - Introduce machine learning scoring
        - Error heatmap
        - Automated alerts
        - Integration deep logs
        - Funnel + performance metrics
        
        ---
        
        # **9. KPI Definitions (for this page only)**
        
        - **Owner Engagement** = Logins in last 30 days
        - **Listing Health** = Photos? Floorplan? EPC?
        - **Conversion Rate** = Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Offers
        - **Revenue Per Owner** = (Stripe charges for services)
        - **Support Load** = # tickets / avg response time
        - **Task Load** = pending tasks linked to owner
        
        ---
        
        # **10. Conversion Funnel (Owner-specific)**
        
        *(Optional Phase 2 section inside this page)*
        
        **Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Offers → Completion**
        
        ---
        
        # **11. Property ID Logic**
        
        Owner detail must also fetch:
        
        - All propertyIDs linked to ownerID
        - All tracking tokens (QR codes, public links)
        
        Also allows admin to search listings by:
        
        - Address
        - Owner email
        - propertyID
        - publicSlug
        
        ---
        
        # **12. Developer Tooling Overview**
        
        - Required tables:
            - owners
            - listings
            - listings_stats
            - viewings
            - inquiries
            - offers
            - billing_events
            - support_tickets
            - tasks
            - system_events
        - Triggers:
            - On new inquiry → add event
            - On new booking → add event
        - Ready for DE expansion (country = “UK” default)

        # **14. Rental Logic (Integrated)**
        
        All data is combined:
        
        - Listings = Sale + Rent
        - Offers = Offers (sale) + Applications (rent)
        - Revenue includes rental service purchases
        - Task types also include landlord services (EICR, gas safety)
        
        No separate screens needed.

    - **🧩 WF-A3 — Home-Hunter Detail View (Admin)**
        
        ---
        
        *(MVP + Phase 2. Mirrors Owner Detail UX for consistency.)*
        
        ```
        ──────────────────────────────
             WF-A3 — HOME-HUNTER DETAIL
        ──────────────────────────────
        ```
        
        This is the Admin’s full CRM-style profile for every buyer/tenant.
        
        ---
        
        # **1. Designer Checklist**
        
        - Use identical layout structure as WF-A2 (Owner Detail)
        - Keep modular: Profile → Offers → Viewings → Saved Places → Surveys → Support
        - Two-column layout on desktop, stacked on mobile
        - Status tags use **Yalla Yellow**
        - Keep it “light” visually — buyers generate more volume than owners
        - Avoid dense tables → use expandable cards
        
        ---
        
        # **2. Developer Checklist**
        
        Admin endpoint needed:
        
        **GET /admin/hunter/{hunterID}**
        
        Must aggregate:
        
        - Profile
        - Contact details
        - KYC / Verification status
        - Saved places
        - Offers made
        - Viewings booked
        - Surveys purchased
        - Support tickets
        - Activity timeline
        - Messages (admin ↔ hunter)
        
        All must support scalable country rollout (UK → DE → …).
        
        ---
        
        # **3. Admin Journey (Short Summary)**
        
        Admin reaches this page via:
        
        - A3 Home-Hunters list
        - Clicking “Buyer profile” inside WF-O3 (Owner Inquiries)
        - Support Inbox ticket related to buyer
        - Offer review (Owner Offer table)
        - Survey purchase logs
        
        This page consolidates **everything about a single Home-Hunter**.
        
        ---
        
        # **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
        
        ```
        A1 Dashboard
           ↓
        A3 Home-Hunters (list)
           ↓ click Hunter
        A3 — Home-Hunter Detail View
           ↓
        Related screens:
           • Offers → WF-O3
           • Surveys → A7
           • Support → A5
           • Viewings → O4 (owner mentions)
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **5. Purpose**
        
        Give Admin a **complete, actionable 360° view** of the buyer/tenant:
        
        - Their position (Cash / Mortgage / Renting)
        - Their reliability (attendance history, cancellations)
        - Offers submitted
        - Viewing behaviour
        - Saved places (interest heatmap)
        - Survey activity
        - Verification status
        - Problems / support threads
        - Fraud signals (Phase 2)
        
        ---
        
        # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
        
        - Identify serious buyers vs browsers
        - Offer transparency for owners/admin
        - Track the buyer journey from interest → booking → offer
        - Flag problematic hunters (no-shows, abuse, spam)
        - Spot upsell opportunities (survey purchase, verification)
        - Ensure safety & compliance
        
        ---
        
        # **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
        
        ## **A. Profile Header Card**
        
        Fields:
        
        - Name
        - Phone
        - Email
        - Buying Position (Cash / Mortgage Ready / In Progress / Browsing)
        - Country (flag)
        - Joined date
        - Last activity
        - Status tags:
            - Verified
            - Unverified
            - High Intent
            - No-Show (x2)
            - Blocked (admin override)
        
        Buttons:
        
        - **Message Home-Hunter**
        - **Block / Unblock User**
        - **Verify / Request Docs**
        
        ---
        
        ## **B. Offers Made**
        
        Table or cards:
        
        | **Place** | **Offer Amount** | **Status** | **Date** | **Owner** | **Action** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        
        Statuses:
        
        - Pending
        - Accepted
        - Rejected
        - Withdrawn
        
        Admin can click → view detailed offer view inside Owner listing.
        
        ---
        
        ## **C. Viewings History**
        
        - Upcoming viewings
        - Past viewings
        - Attendance score (Phase 2)
        
        Example:
        
        | **Place** | **Type** | **Date** | **Attended?** | **Notes** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        
        ---
        
        ## **D. Saved Places (Wishlist)**
        
        This shows where the Home-Hunter’s **interest is strongest**.
        
        Clickable cards linking to WF-O5 (Public Property Page).
        
        Each card has:
        
        - Thumbnail
        - Address
        - Price
        - “Last viewed”
        - “Favourite since…”
        
        ---
        
        ## **E. Surveys Purchased**
        
        Table:
        
        | **Property** | **Survey Date** | **Price Paid** | **Download** | **Status** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        
        Future (Phase 2):
        
        - Resale earnings
        - Survey expiry
        - Verification status
        
        ---
        
        ## **F. Verification (KYC)**
        
        For making offers & serious activity.
        
        Fields:
        
        - ID document (link)
        - Proof of funds
        - Mortgage in Principle (PDF)
        - Verification Status (Pending / Approved / Rejected)
        - Notes (Admin)
        
        ---
        
        ## **G. Support History**
        
        List of all support interactions:
        
        - Open tickets
        - Closed tickets
        - Last message
            
            Links to A5 (Support Inbox).
            
        
        ---
        
        ## **H. Activity Timeline**
        
        A chronological “all events” feed:
        
        - Saved a place
        - Booked a viewing
        - Viewed property page
        - Made an offer
        - Uploaded document
        - Purchased survey
        - Support ticket opened
        
        ---
        
        # **8. Developer Requirements**
        
        ### **Tables to join:**
        
        - hunters
        - hunter_profiles
        - inquiries
        - offers
        - viewings
        - saved_places
        - surveys_purchased
        - support_tickets
        - system_events
        - verification_documents
        
        ### **MVP logic:**
        
        - Minimal KYC (photo ID only)
        - No fraud detection
        - Simple offer tracking
        - Basic timeline using system_events
        
        ### **Phase 2 logic:**
        
        - Attendance scoring
        - Fraud scoring (device mismatch, rapid activity bursts)
        - Automated identity verification
        - Offer escalation engine
        - Behaviour insights (heatmaps)
        
        ---
        
        # **9. KPI Definitions (for HH-specific page)**
        
        - **Intent Score** = # viewings + offers + survey purchases
        - **Attendance Rate** = attended / booked
        - **Interest Spread** = number of saved places
        - **Offer Quality** = average offer-to-asking ratio
        - **Survey Engagement** = surveys purchased / viewed listings
        - **Verification Level** = 0–3 scale (unverified → fully verified)
        
        ---
        
        # **10. Conversion Funnel (HH-specific)**
        
        **Saved Place → Viewing Booked → Viewing Attended → Offer Made → Offer Accepted**
        
        Displayed only in Phase 2.
        
        ---
        
        # **11. Property ID Logic**
        
        Home-Hunters link to listings by:
        
        - propertyID
        - publicSlug
        - QR token (from signboard scan)
        - inquiryID
        - offerID
        - viewingID
        
        Admin must be able to click into each.
        
        ---
        
        # **12. Developer Tooling Overview**
        
        - Same components used in Owner Detail
        - Reuse ActivityFeed, TaskPanel, SupportPreview
        - Add VerificationPanel component
        - Add OfferHistory table
        - Add SavedPlaces list
        - Add SurveyHistory table
        
        ---

        # **14. Rental Logic (Integrated)**
        
        For renters:
        
        - Offers become **Applications**
        - Proof of funds replaced with **References**
        - Mortgage documents disabled
        - Saved places identical
        - Viewings identical
        - KYC simplified
        
        No separate wireframe needed.

    - **🧩 WF-A4 — Integrations & Status (Admin Control Panel)**
        
        *(MVP + Phase 2. Shows health of all external systems.)*
        
        ```
        ────────────────────────────────
             WF-A4 — INTEGRATIONS & STATUS
        ────────────────────────────────
        ```
        
        # **1. Designer Checklist**
        
        - Use Dashfolio+ **card grid layout**
        - Use consistent icon style (simple outline icons)
        - Health states must be visually distinct:
            - 🟢 Connected
            - 🟡 Warning
            - 🔴 Error
            - ⚪ Coming Soon (inactive services)
        - Each integration card should be clickable → open detailed log modal
        - Provide space for short description + last sync timestamp
        - Keep layout expandable (Phase 2 brings more integrations)
        
        ---
        
        # **2. Developer Checklist**
        
        ### **MVP:**
        
        - Build /admin/integrations/status endpoint
        - Return real status for:
            - Stripe
            - Twilio WhatsApp API
            - Email (SendGrid or Mailgun)
            - Calendar Sync (Google API)
        - Display placeholder cards for:
            - Rightmove
            - Zoopla
            - OnTheMarket
            - Facebook Marketplace
        
        ### **Phase 2:**
        
        - Add webhook log viewer
        - Add auto-retry buttons
        - Add error-log filters
        - Add integration setup wizards for country expansion
        
        ---
        
        # **3. Admin Journey (Short Summary)**
        
        This page is accessed when:
        
        - The dashboard shows an alert (A1 → A4)
        - A support ticket reports a booking failure
        - A viewing sync fails
        - Stripe revenue looks off
        - Listings fail to publish to portals (Phase 2)
        
        A4 is the **central system health monitor**.
        
        ---
        
        # **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
        
        ```
        A1 Dashboard
           ↓ Alerts → Integration Issues
        A4 — Integrations & Status
           ↓
        View Logs / Fix Issues / Retry Sync
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **5. Purpose**
        
        Provide Admin with a **single page** to verify all key integrations:
        
        - Messaging
        - Payments
        - Email
        - Calendar
        - Property portals
        - Maps
        - Authentication services
        - External data enrichments (Phase 2)
        
        This prevents chaos when something breaks.
        
        ---
        
        # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
        
        - Quickly identify issues
        - Understand why something failed (logs)
        - Retry actions
        - Check syncing reliability
        - Keep owners & hunters informed
        - Avoid downtime or missed viewings
        - Provide transparency for support team
        
        ---
        
        # **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
        
        ## **A. Integration Status Grid**
        
        ## **(top section)**
        
        Each card includes:
        
        - Integration Name
        - Icon
        - Status indicator
        - Short description
        - Timestamp: “Last Sync: X min ago”
        - CTA:
            - **View Logs** (modal)
            - **Retry** (if error state — Phase 2)
        
        ### **MVP Integrations (Active)**
        
        - **Stripe Payments** — 🟢/🟡/🔴
        - **Twilio WhatsApp API** — 🟢/🟡/🔴
        - **Email Provider (SendGrid)** — 🟢/🟡/🔴
        - **Google Calendar Sync** — 🟢/🟡/🔴
        - **Maps (Mapbox or Google Maps)** — 🟢/🟡/🔴
        
        ### **Placeholder Integrations (Phase 2 — show “coming soon”)**
        
        - Rightmove Real-Time Feed
        - Zoopla
        - OnTheMarket
        - Facebook Marketplace
        - Germany-specific portals (ImmoScout24, Immowelt)
        
        ---
        
        ## **B. Error Log Panel**
        
        A collapsible panel showing last 10 errors:
        
        | **Time** | **Integration** | **Error** | **Action** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        | 12:14 | WhatsApp | Rate limit exceeded | Retry |
        | 11:03 | Email | API key expired | Update Key |
        | 10:22 | Calendar | OAuth failed | Reconnect |
        
        **MVP:** View only
        
        **Phase 2:** Retry + filter + export logs
        
        ---
        
        ## **C. Integration Detail Modal**
        
        (Clicking “View Logs” from a card)
        
        Shows:
        
        - Success/Fail events
        - Response codes
        - Triggered actions
        - Error messages
        - Retry history
        - Webhook payload (Phase 2)
        - Setup instructions (nice for onboarding)
        
        ---
        
        ## **D. Setup & Credentials Section (Phase 2)**
        
        Grouped inputs:
        
        - API keys
        - Secrets
        - Webhook URLs
        - OAuth reconnect buttons
        - Region settings
        
        ### **Important:**
        
        **Do NOT show full API keys.**
        
        Use masked fields (•••••••).
        
        ---
        
        # **8. Developer Requirements**
        
        ### **MVP version:**
        
        - Basic integration checks
        - Check availability via “ping” or test endpoint
        - Store logs in:
            - integration_logs
            - system_logs (fallback)
        - Error messages should be safe (no secrets)
        - Use cron jobs for automated health polling (every 30–60 min)
        
        ### **Phase 2:**
        
        - Full-event log storage
        - Webhook replay
        - Auto-retry
        - Multi-country (UK/DE) integration selection
        - Alerts sent to Admin via WhatsApp
        
        ---
        
        # **9. KPI Definitions (Integration Health)**
        
        | **KPI** | **Definition** |
        | --- | --- |
        | Uptime % | Successful checks / total checks |
        | Failure Rate | Errors in last 24h |
        | Message Delivery Rate | WhatsApp sent/delivered |
        | Email Bounce Rate | Bounce / total |
        | Successful Bookings | Calendar sync reliability |
        | Payment Success Rate | Stripe charges succeeded |
        
        This becomes part of A1 (Admin Dashboard) in Phase 2.
        
        ---
        
        # **10. Conversion Funnel (Integration Reliability)**
        
        *(Phase 2 only)*
        
        WhatsApp → Email → Calendar → Offer
        
        Tracks where drops happen.
        
        ---
        
        # **11. Property ID Logic**
        
        Not directly used here, but integration logs **must reference**:
        
        - propertyID
        - ownerID
        - hunterID
        - actionID
        - listingSlug
        
        So Admin can trace errors like:
        
        - “Calendar sync failed for viewing #2323”
        - “WhatsApp message failed for inquiry #1234”
        
        ---
        
        # **12. Developer Tooling Overview**
        
        - Required tables:
            - integration_status
            - integration_logs
            - system_logs
            - errors
            - support_tickets
        - External dependencies:
            - Stripe
            - Twilio
            - SendGrid
            - Google API (auth + calendar)
            - Mapbox / Google Maps
        - Phase 2:
            - Rightmove API
            - Zoopla API
            - OnTheMarket feed
            - Germany portals (ImmoScout24, Immowelt)

    - **🧩 WF-A5 — Buyer Detail View (Admin)**
        
        ---
        
        This is the Admin’s single place to understand a **Home-Hunter’s full profile, activity, verification status, offers, viewings, and linked surveys**.
        
        # **1. Designer Checklist**
        
        - Use Dashfolio+ standard page layout
        - Keep everything in **modular cards** (stacked in 2-column layout)
        - Show “Buyer Status Bar” at top (verification + buying position)
        - Important: Activity cards must be visually distinct:
            - Viewings
            - Offers
            - Surveys
            - Messages
        - Add icons for clarity (but keep outline style)
        - Ensure responsive design for laptop-sized admin workstations
        
        ---
        
        # **2. Developer Checklist**
        
        ### **MVP:**
        
        - Endpoint: /admin/buyer/:buyerID
        - Pull structured data:
            - Profile
            - Contact (masked partially)
            - Buying Position
            - Viewings history
            - Booked upcoming viewings
            - Offers submitted
            - Surveys purchased / uploaded
            - Messages (inquiry history)
            - Device info (optional MVP)
        - Cross-link to:
            - WF-A2 (Owner Detail View) if they interacted with an owner
        - Mask sensitive fields (GDPR-safe)
        - Log admin actions
        
        ### **Phase 2:**
        
        - KYC verification module
        - Document validation (proof of funds, ID, etc.)
        - Offer comparison analytics
        - Fraud detection markers
        - “Buyer Quality Score”
        
        ---
        
        # **3. Admin Journey (Short Summary)**
        
        Admin arrives here when:
        
        - A buyer sends an offer
        - There is a suspicious activity report
        - A survey was purchased but failed payment
        - Owner flags a buyer (rude, spam, trolling)
        - Buyer needs support with booking
        - Buyer verification/KYC pending
        
        This view combines everything in one place.
        
        ---
        
        # **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
        
        ```
        Admin Sidebar
           ↓
        A1 — Dashboard
           ↓ click: Buyer Activity / Offers
        A5 — Buyer Detail View
           ↓
        View → Fix → Support → Verify → Log Note
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **5. Purpose**
        
        Give the Admin a 360° view of a home-hunter:
        
        - identity & verification
        - communication history
        - viewing behaviour
        - offers submitted
        - financial readiness
        - surveys and marketplace activity
        - compliance flags
        - account insights (login behaviour, device, IP)
        
        It’s the *“CRM profile”* of the buyer.
        
        ---
        
        # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
        
        - Who is this buyer? (Name, phone, email)
        - Can they afford the property? (Buying position)
        - Are they serious or browsing?
        - Do they have upcoming viewings?
        - Have they ghosted owners?
        - Did they upload required documents?
        - Are they verified?
        - Are they problematic (owner flagged)?
        - Do they need support / follow-up?
        
        Admin should be able to act fast.
        
        ---
        
        # **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
        
        ### **A. Buyer Header Bar (Top)**
        
        Contains:
        
        - **Name**
        - Buying Position badge:
            - ✔ Cash Buyer
            - ✔ Mortgage in Principle
            - ⏳ Mortgage in Progress
            - 👀 Just Browsing
        - Verification Status badge:
            - 🔵 Basic
            - 🟢 Verified
            - 🔴 Flagged
        - Contact info:
            - Phone
            - Email
            - Preferred communication: WhatsApp/Email
        
        ---
        
        ### **B. Profile Details Card**
        
        - Name
        - Email (masked partially)
        - Phone number
        - Country
        - Created at
        - Last active
        - Device info (optional MVP)
        
        Admin actions:
        
        - Resend verification link
        - Disable account
        - Flag buyer
        
        ---
        
        ### **C. Viewings Card**
        
        **Upcoming Viewings**
        
        Tabular:
        
        | **Date** | **Time** | **Place** | **Owner** | **Status** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        | 12 Mar | 14:00 | 12 King St | John S. | Confirmed |
        
        **Past Viewings**
        
        With feedback flag.
        
        ---
        
        ### **D. Offers Card**
        
        List of offers:
        
        | **Date** | **Place** | **£ Offer** | **Status** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        | 10 Mar | 12 King St | £512,000 | Under Review |
        | 02 Mar | 5 Elm Rd | £490,000 | Rejected |
        
        Admin can open offer → go to Owner view.
        
        ---
        
        ### **E. Messages / Inquiries Card**
        
        Conversation history:
        
        | **Date** | **Owner** | **Message Type** | **Status** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        | 10 Mar | John S. | Viewing Q | Replied |
        | 09 Mar | Sarah T. | Offer | Open |
        
        Click → open WF-A7 Support Inbox for full thread.
        
        ---
        
        ### **F. Survey Marketplace Card**
        
        Tracks whether buyer:
        
        - Uploaded surveys
        - Purchased surveys
        - Shared surveys
        - Earned credits (Phase 2)
        
        Table:
        
        | **Property** | **Type** | **Date** | **Status** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        | 12 King St | RICS Level 2 | 09 Mar | Purchased |
        
        ---
        
        ### **G. Flags & Notes Card**
        
        Admin-only notes:
        
        - Owner complaints
        - Behaviour warnings
        - Fraud suspicion markers
        - Manual priority rating
        
        ---
        
        ### **H. Action Bar (Bottom)**
        
        Buttons:
        
        - Send WhatsApp
        - Send Email
        - Add Admin Note
        - Export Buyer Data (GDPR)
        - Disable Account
        - Verify Buyer
        
        ---
        
        # **8. Developer Requirements**
        
        ### **Data sources required:**
        
        - buyers
        - buyer_activity
        - buyer_viewings
        - buyer_offers
        - buyer_messages
        - surveys
        - admin_notes
        - flags
        
        ### **Actions:**
        
        - Mask PII
        - Log admin interactions
        - Allow safe export on request
        - Link with WF-A1, A2, A7
        
        ---
        
        # **9. KPI Definitions**
        
        Admin sees:
        
        # **Total viewings booked**
        
        # **Offers submitted**
        
        - Offer acceptance %
        - Average offer vs asking price
        - Survey earnings
        - No-show rate
        - Response rate
        
        These feed into the global KPI dashboard (A9).
        
        ---
        
        # **10. Conversion Funnel (Buyer-Focused)**
        
        ```
        Viewing Booked
              ↓
        Viewing Attended
              ↓
        Offer Submitted
              ↓
        Offer Negotiation
              ↓
        Sale Completed (Owner workflow)
        ```
        
        Admin sees which buyers are “cold / warm / hot.”
        
        ---
        
        # **11. ID Logic**
        
        Each record references:
        
        - buyerID
        - placeID
        - ownerID
        - offerID
        - viewingID
        - surveyID
        
        Ensures trackability across the system.
        
        ---
        
        # **12. Developer Tooling**
        
        - Must include buyer_history endpoint
        - Build buyer_profile_view() method
        - Use indexed search by phone/email
        - Store flag reasons for audit trail
        - Provide admin export for GDPR

        ---
        
    - **🧩 WF-A6 — Survey Marketplace Oversight (Admin)**
        
        ---
        
        - how buyers behave (they commission the survey)
        - how owners behave (they WANT surveys shown)
        - how marketplaces generate revenue (two-sided marketplace)
        - how we want to scale across markets (UK → Germany → global)
        
        ---
        
        # **1. Designer Checklist**
        
        - Dashfolio+ layout
        - Use two main tabs:
            - **Uploaded Surveys (Pending Review)**
            - **Live Marketplace (Approved)**
            - **Purchases & Earnings**
        - Owner uploads and HH uploads must be visually distinct:
            - Owner Upload → blue tag
            - Hunter Upload → green tag
        - Survey preview modal (PDF viewer)
        - Use chips: Pending / Approved / Rejected / Flagged
        - Add “Show on Listing (Owner toggle)” indicator
        - Include link: “Open Listing”
        - Include link: “Open Home-Hunter” (if HH uploaded)
        
        ---
        
        # **2. Developer Checklist**
        
        ### **Data Model Requirements**
        
        - surveys (core table)
        - survey_uploads (uploadID)
        - survey_status
        - survey_sales
        - survey_property_links (placeID → surveyID)
        - survey_origin (owner or home-hunter)
        - survey_visibility (public / owner-hidden)
        
        ### **API Requirements**
        
        - Review: Approve / Reject / Flag
        - Link/unlink survey to property
        - Toggle “Show on Listing”
        - Set price
        - Trigger payout
        - Issue refund
        
        ### **Validation**
        
        - PDF only
        - Size < 20MB
        - Virus scan (recommended)
        - Address match logic (optional Phase 2)
        
        ---
        
        # **3. Admin Journey (Short Summary)**
        
        Admin enters the page when:
        
        - A survey was uploaded by **Owner** or **Home-Hunter**
        - A survey is waiting for approval
        - A survey is flagged
        - A survey was purchased
        - Payout needs triggering
        - Owner reports incorrect survey
        - Home-Hunter requests dispute
        - Survey visibility must be corrected on listing
        
        Admin acts as the **central quality gatekeeper**.
        
        ---
        
        # **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
        
        ```
        Admin Sidebar
            ↓
        Survey Marketplace (A6)
            ↓
        Review → Approve → Publish → Sell → Payout
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **5. Purpose**
        
        Enable Yalla.House to:
        
        - Control survey quality
        - Protect buyers from fraudulent files
        - Allow owners to upload proactively
        - Allow home-hunters to earn money
        - Boost trust & transparency in property listings
        - Improve offer rate & speed
        - Increase marketplace revenue
        
        This is a key differentiator vs Rightmove/Zoopla.
        
        ---
        
        # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
        
        - Which surveys are pending review?
        - Which belong to Owners vs Home-Hunters?
        - Which surveys are approved & generating revenue?
        - Which ones have visibility enabled on the listing?
        - Which buyers bought which surveys?
        - Who needs payout?
        - Are there disputes?
        - Are properties missing surveys that could speed up sale?
        
        ---
        
        # **7. Designer: What to Build in Framer**
        
        ## **7.1 Top KPI Row (cards)**
        
        - Total Surveys Uploaded
        - Surveys Approved
        - Pending Approval
        - Survey Purchases
        - Revenue (Marketplace)
        - Payouts Due
        - Disputes Open
        
        ---
        
        ## **7.2 Tab 1 — Uploaded Surveys (Pending Review)**
        
        Table:
        
        | Survey ID | Uploaded By | Role (Owner/HH) | Property | Date | Type | Status | Actions |
        
        Actions:
        
        - Review (PDF modal)
        - Approve
        - Reject
        - Flag
        - Link to property
        - Add admin note
        
        Filters:
        
        - Owner uploads
        - HH uploads
        - Type
        - Property
        - Status
        
        **Survey Preview Modal**
        
        - PDF viewer
        - Property address
        - Upload origin (owner/hunter)
        - Uploader info
        - Notes
        - Approve / Reject / Flag
        
        ---
        
        ## **7.3 Tab 2 — Live Marketplace (Approved)**
        
        Table:
        
        | Survey | Property | Visible on Listing? | Upload Origin | Price | Purchased | Earnings | Actions |
        
        Actions:
        
        - Change price
        - Toggle “Show on Listing”
        - Suspend survey
        - Payout uploader
        - View purchase log
        
        ---
        
        ## **7.4 Tab 3 — Purchases & Earnings**
        
        Table:
        
        | Purchase ID | Survey ID | Buyer | Property | Price | Payout | Status | Date |
        
        Statuses:
        
        - Completed
        - Pending payout
        - Refunded
        - Disputed
        
        Admin actions:
        
        - Trigger payout
        - Refund buyer
        - Open dispute window
        
        ---
        
        # **8. Developer Requirements**
        
        ### **Hybrid Upload Logic**
        
        - Owners can upload surveys
        - Home-Hunters can upload surveys
        - Both follow same approval workflow
        - Surveys attach to property via placeID
        
        ### **Survey Visibility Rules**
        
        - Owner chooses “show/hide”
        - Admin override allowed
        - Default = visible
        
        ### **Marketplace Revenue Model**
        
        - Price set by admin
        - Revenue split:
            - Default 50% HH / 50% Yalla
            - Owner uploads → 100% to Yalla or Owner?
                
                ✔ Recommend: **Owner uploads = Yalla keeps 100%** (no commission to Owner; file is free for Owner)
                
        
        ### **Audit Requirements**
        
        Log:
        
        - Who uploaded
        - Who approved
        - When price was changed
        - Every payout
        - Every refund
        - Dispute trails
        
        ---
        
        # **9. KPI Definitions**
        
        - Approval rate
        - Marketplace revenue
        - Uploader revenue (HH)
        - Survey reuse rate
        - Surveys per property
        - Visibility enabled %
        - Dispute rate
        - Suspicious upload rate
        
        ---
        
        # **10. Hybrid Survey Funnel (FINAL)**
        
        ```
        Owner Uploads Survey (optional)
                       OR
        Home-Hunter Uploads Survey (after paying)
        
        ↓
        Admin Review & Approval
        ↓
        Survey becomes:
           - Visible on Listing
           - Available on Marketplace
        ↓
        Buyer purchases survey
        ↓
        Uploader earns → Yalla earns
        ↓
        Owner benefits from more confident offers
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **11. ID Logic**
        
        - surveyID
        - uploadID
        - hunterID (if HH upload)
        - ownerID (if Owner upload)
        - propertyID
        - purchaseID
        - payoutID
        - disputeID
        
        ---
        
        # **12. Developer Tooling Overview**
        
        - Stripe Connect payouts
        - Secure PDF storage (S3)
        - Virus scanning
        - Survey linking logic
        - Visibility toggles
        - Cron job for automated payouts
        - Audit log
        
        ---
        
        # **13. Dummy Content**
        
        ```
        Survey ID: S-00491
        Uploaded by: Owner (Oliver R.)
        ```
