- 
- design the **HH Gate modal copy**, or
- map **email / WhatsApp confirmations for bookings**.

Just tell me where to go next.

- Home Hunter Data Model
    
    ```jsx
    HomeHunter {
      id: string (UUID)
      createdAt: timestamp
      updatedAt: timestamp
    
      // Basic profile
      name: string
      email: string
      phone: string
      phoneVerified: boolean
      buyingPosition: enum[
        "cash",
        "mortgage_ready",
        "mortgage_in_progress",
        "just_browsing"
      ]
      country: string
      verifiedAt: timestamp | null
    
      // Viewing activity
      savedProperties: [propertyID]
      viewingsRequested: [viewingRequestID]
      viewingsConfirmed: [viewingID]
    
      // Communication
      inquiries: [inquiryID]
      ownerMessagesCount: number
    
      // Funnel
      funnelStage: enum[
        "anonymous",
        "profile_started",
        "phone_sent",
        "phone_verified",
        "gate_completed"
      ]
    }
    ```
    
- **Public → HH → Message Owner**,
    
    
- **📞📩  Contact & Communication Workflows (MASTER TABLES)**
    1. **Who contacts NoAgent**
    2. **Through which channel**
    3. **What automation happens**
    4. **Which workflow is triggered**
    5. **Which external services are required**
    6. **What wireframes are involved**
    
    This is written so **Designer, Developer, and Ops** all read the *same truth*.
    
    ---
    
    ## **TABLE 1 — Contact Entry Points → Workflow Resolution**
    
    | **#** | **Contact Type** | **Entry Channel** | **Initial Trigger** | **System Action** | **Final Destination** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | 1 | Home-Hunter | Portal click (Rightmove/Zoopla) | Click listing URL | Resolve Place ID → redirect | WF-O5 Public Property Page |
    | 2 | Home-Hunter | Portal call (generic number) | Phone call | Auto-SMS resolver | WF-O5 via Place ID |
    | 3 | Home-Hunter | Portal email | Email enquiry | Auto-reply with link | WF-O5 |
    | 4 | Home-Hunter | WhatsApp | WhatsApp CTA / message | Pre-filled link | WF-O5 |
    | 5 | Home-Hunter | QR code (signboard) | Scan QR | Direct resolve | WF-O5 |
    | 6 | Home-Hunter | Word of mouth | Manual search | Site search | WF-O5 |
    | 7 | Owner | Website CTA | “List your place” | Login / Magic link | WF-O2 Wizard |
    | 8 | Owner | Email | Support / onboarding | Manual / ticket | Account / Support |
    | 9 | Partner / Agent | Services page | Inquiry form | CRM / email | WF-P7 (Service Provider) |
    | 10 | Admin | Internal tools | Dashboard action | Manual / automated | WF-A1–A9 |
    
    ---
    
    ## **TABLE 2 — Home-Hunter Communication Workflows (DETAILED)**
    
    | **Channel** | **Trigger** | **Automated Message / Action** | **User Response** | **Outcome** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | SMS | HH calls generic number | “Reply with postcode or address to get booking link” | Address / postcode | Resolve → send WF-O5 link |
    | SMS | Multiple matches | “Reply 1 or 2” | Selection | Correct listing link |
    | SMS | No match | “We couldn’t find that property” | Retry | Fallback to site |
    | WhatsApp | HH clicks CTA | Pre-filled message with link | Optional reply | HH lands on WF-O5 |
    | Email | Portal enquiry | Auto-reply with booking link | Click link | WF-O5 |
    | Web | Booking attempt | Verification modal | Complete profile | WF-H1 Booking |
    
    ---
    
    ## **TABLE 3 — Owner Communication Workflows**
    
    | **Trigger** | **Channel** | **Message / Action** | **External Service** | **Owner UI** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | New inquiry | Email | “New inquiry received” | Email (SendGrid) | WF-O3 |
    | Viewing booked | Email | Booking confirmation | Email | WF-O4 |
    | Viewing request (no slots) | Email | “Viewing requested” | Email | WF-O3 / WF-O4 |
    | Calendar sync | API | Create calendar event | Google Calendar API | WF-O4 |
    | Listing shared | QR / Link | Static link | — | WF-O5 Preview |
    
    ---
    
    ## **TABLE 4 — Communication Actions by Wireframe**
    
    | **Wireframe** | **Action** | **Communication** | **Service Needed** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | WF-O1 Dashboard | Activity alerts | Email summary (Phase 2) | Email |
    | WF-O2 Wizard | Listing creation | — | — |
    | WF-O3 Inquiries | Message HH | In-app + email fallback | Email |
    | WF-O4 Calendar | Booking confirmation | Email | Email |
    | WF-O5 Public Page | Book / Request viewing | Verification + booking | SMS / Email |
    | WF-H1 Booking | Slot confirmation | Email | Email |
    | WF-A4 Integrations | Status monitoring | — | — |
    
    ---
    
    ## **TABLE 5 — External Services Required (Phase 1)**
    
    | **Service** | **Purpose** | **Used In** | **Required Phase** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | **Twilio (SMS + Voice)** | Call capture, SMS resolver | Portal calls, QR fallback | Phase 1 |
    | **WhatsApp (via Twilio or Meta)** | HH messaging | WhatsApp CTA | Phase 1 |
    | **Email (SendGrid / Postmark)** | Notifications, auto-replies | All workflows | Phase 1 |
    | **Google Calendar API** | Owner calendar sync | WF-O4 | Phase 1 |
    | **Feed Aggregator** | Portal publishing | Rightmove / Zoopla | Phase 1 |
    | **QR Code Generator** | Signboards | Owner tools | Phase 1 |
    | **Analytics (GA / internal)** | Attribution | All | Phase 1 |
    | **CRM / Ticketing** | Support & partners | Admin | Phase 2 |
    
    ---
    
    ## **TABLE 6 — Automation Copy (Ready to Use)**
    
    | **Channel** | **Situation** | **Copy** |
    | --- | --- | --- |
    | SMS | After call | “Thanks for calling about a NoAgent listing. Reply with the postcode or street + number to get the booking link.” |
    | SMS | Success | “Here’s the listing and live availability: https://noagent.global/p/{placeId}” |
    | WhatsApp | Prefill | “Hi, I’m interested in this property: https://noagent.global/p/{placeId}” |
    | Email | Auto-reply | “Thanks for your interest. View details and book a viewing here: https://noagent.global/p/{placeId}” |
    | UI | Locked CTA | “Verify your profile to continue.” |
    
    ---
    
    ## **TABLE 7 — Wireframes That Must Reflect These Workflows**
    
    | **Wireframe** | **Required Update** |
    | --- | --- |
    | WF-O2 Wizard | “Listing created after Step 1” microcopy |
    | WF-O5 Owner Preview | “All links point here” microcopy |
    | WF-O3 Inquiries | Source + contact method labels |
    | WF-O4 Calendar | Viewing requests vs bookings |
    | WF-A4 Integrations | Phone / SMS / WhatsApp status |
    | WF-P7 Services | Partner inquiry routing |
    
    ---
    
    ## **🔒 FINAL LOCK — Communications Architecture**
    
    > All inbound contacts (portal, phone, WhatsApp, SMS, email, QR, word of mouth) are resolved to a Place ID before any action occurs.
    > 
    
    > Automated communications guide Home-Hunters to the Public Property Page (WF-O5), where booking is the primary action.
    > 
    
    > External services are modular, minimal, and Phase-1 safe.
    >

    3. Finalise **WF-H1 Home-Hunter Booking Flow**

### **Home Hunters**

- Home Hunter Funnel
    
    Below is the **sanity-check of the Public → Home-Hunter → Booking flow**, with **clear ownership of pages, states, and responsibilities**.
    
    ---
    
    # **Public → Home-Hunter → Booking**
    
    ---
    
    ## **0️⃣ Where this flow lives (important framing)**
    
    This flow **does NOT live on WF-P1**.
    
    It lives across **three page types**:
    
    | **Stage** | **Page** | **Owner** |
    | --- | --- | --- |
    | Discovery | **WF-P6 — Public Property Page** | Public |
    | Intent & gating | **Inline modal / drawer** | Public → HH |
    | Action | **WF-H3 — My Bookings** | Home-Hunter |
    
    👉 **WF-P6 is the anchor**
    
    Everything starts there.
    
    ---
    
    ## **1️⃣ Entry: Public Discovery**
    
    ### **Entry points (all covered)**
    
    A Home-Hunter arrives via:
    
    - Property portal (Rightmove / ImmoScout / etc.)
    - QR code on sign
    - WhatsApp / SMS link
    - Shared direct link
    - Search on NoAgent (later)
    
    👉 All routes land on:
    
    **WF-P6 — Public Property Page**
    
    ---
    
    ## **2️⃣ Public Property Page (WF-P6)**
    
    ### **What the Home-Hunter sees**
    
    - Full property details
    - Photos, description, map
    - Prominent **Book a viewing** CTA
    - Secondary actions:
        - Message owner
        - Save place
    
    ### **Sanity checks**
    
    - ✅ No login required to browse
    - ✅ Booking is the *primary* action
    - ✅ Page feels trustworthy and complete
    
    **Pass condition:**
    
    HH understands the property and wants to act.
    
    ---
    
    ## **3️⃣ Action Click: “Book a viewing”**
    
    ### **What happens next (critical)**
    
    👉 **Inline HH Gate opens**
    
    (Not a new page)
    
    This can be:
    
    - Modal
    - Drawer
    - Full-screen on mobile
    
    ---
    
    ## **4️⃣ Home-Hunter Gate (Inline)**
    
    This replaces the classic “agent phone call”.
    
    ### **Minimum required info (Phase 1)**
    
    | **Field** | **Why** |
    | --- | --- |
    | Name | Human contact |
    | Email | Confirmation |
    | Phone | Verification |
    | Buy or Rent | Context |
    | Position | Quality signal |
    
    Examples:
    
    - Cash buyer
    - Mortgage in principle
    - Employed renter
    - Student / guarantor
    
    ### **Sanity checks**
    
    - ✅ Only asked **once**
    - ✅ No account jargon
    - ✅ Clear reason given:
        
        > “Owners need basic details to confirm viewings.”
        > 
    
    **Pass condition:**
    
    HH feels this is normal, not intrusive.
    
    ---
    
    ## **5️⃣ Verification (Light)**
    
    - SMS code (if phone entered)
    - Or email link (fallback)
    
    👉 Still **inside the booking flow**, not a separate “signup”.
    
    ---
    
    ## **6️⃣ Slot Selection (Still WF-P6 context)**
    
    ### **If slots exist**
    
    - Calendar picker appears
    - HH selects time
    - Confirms booking
    
    ### **If no slots exist**
    
    - HH sees:
        
        > “No slots available right now”
        > 
    - Can:
        - Request a viewing
        - Leave availability note
    
    Owner is notified.
    
    ---
    
    ## **7️⃣ Confirmation & Transition**
    
    After booking is confirmed:
    
    ### **HH sees:**
    
    - Confirmation message
    - Calendar details
    - “View your bookings” CTA
    
    👉 This is where **HH officially exists**
    
    ---
    
    ## **8️⃣ Where does the HH land next?**
    
    👉 **WF-H3 — My Bookings**
    
    This is the HH’s **home base**, not a dashboard.
    
    ### **Why not WF-H1 first?**
    
    - Booking is the intent
    - Bookings page confirms success
    - Avoids empty dashboards
    
    **WF-H1 (Dashboard)** can be introduced later as a summary.
    
    ---
    
    ## **9️⃣ Post-booking behaviour**
    
    From **WF-H3 — My Bookings**, HH can:
    
    - See upcoming view
    - Message owner (thread already created)
    - Cancel / reschedule (rules apply)
    - Upload documents later (Phase 2)
    
    ---
    
    ## **🔒 Key Sanity Rules (you are following them)**
    
    - ❌ No forced signup page
    - ❌ No generic HH dashboard before intent
    - ❌ No booking without property context
    - ✅ Booking is property-bound
    - ✅ HH account is created *as a side-effect of action*
    - ✅ This mirrors real-world agent behaviour
    
    ---
    
    ## **📍 One-sentence answer to your question**
    
    > Public → Home-Hunter → Booking sits primarily on WF-P6,
    > 
    
    > with an inline Home-Hunter gate, and transitions into WF-H3 after confirmation.
    > 
    
    That’s the cleanest, lowest-friction architecture.
    
    ---
    
    ## **✅ Verdict**
    
    ✔ Flow is natural
    
    ✔ Trust-preserving
    
    ✔ Conversion-optimised
    
    ✔ Easy to explain to designers and developers
    
    ✔ Scales across countries and portals
    
    ---
    
- **Home-Hunter Preferences (WF-H1)** & Inbox Rules (WF-H2)
    - **🔁 Owner ↔ Home-Hunter ↔ Agent**
    **End-to-End Flow (Phase 1 — Locked)**
        
        ---
        
        ## **🧑‍💼 1. OWNER FLOW (Listing → Viewings → Optional Agent)**
        
        ### **O1 — Owner lists a property**
        
        - Owner completes **WF-O2 (Listing Wizard)**
        - Property ID is created
        - Owner sets:
            - Viewing availability
            - Confirmation mode (manual default)
        - Listing goes live (own site + portals if enabled)
        
        ---
        
        ### **O2 — Owner receives Home-Hunter activity**
        
        - All HH actions appear in:
            - **WF-O1 (Dashboard)** → KPIs
            - **WF-O3 (Inquiries & Offers)** → Inbox
        - Owner sees:
            - HH verification status
            - Booking requests
            - Messages
        
        ---
        
        ### **O3 — Owner decision point: involve an agent (OPTIONAL)**
        
        Owner may choose to:
        
        - handle everything themselves **(default)**
        - OR ask for agent help
        
        If Owner clicks **“Find agents in my area”**:
        
        - Opens agent discovery (read-only)
        - Postcode auto-filled
        - Owner can send **context-rich request**:
            
            > “I’ve listed my property on NoAgent and may need help with viewings / negotiation.”
            > 
        
        ➡️ Owner stays in control.
        
        ➡️ No agent can contact Owner unless Owner initiates.
        
        ---
        
        ## **🧍 2. HOME-HUNTER FLOW (Discover → Book → Decide)**
        
        ### **H1 — HH discovers property**
        
        Entry points:
        
        - NoAgent site
        - Portal (Rightmove / ImmoScout / etc.)
        - QR code on sign
        - WhatsApp / SMS auto-reply
        - Word of mouth link
        
        All routes lead to:
        
        👉 **WF-O5 / WF-P6 — Public Property Page**
        
        ---
        
        ### **H2 — HH primary actions**
        
        From the property page, HH can:
        
        - Request / book a viewing
        - Message Owner
        - Save property
        
        **Before first contact**, HH must pass:
        
        👉 **HH Gate (profile + verification)**
        
        This creates:
        
        - HH account
        - Preferences (WF-H1)
        - Inbox (WF-H2)
        
        ---
        
        ### **H3 — HH booking logic**
        
        - If Owner = manual confirmation:
            - HH sees **“Request viewing”**
            - Status = pending
        - If auto-confirm:
            - HH sees **“Book instantly”**
            - Slot confirmed immediately
        
        HH sees all bookings in:
        
        👉 **WF-H3 — My Bookings**
        
        ---
        
        ### **H4 — HH decides to involve agents (OPTIONAL)**
        
        From:
        
        - **WF-H1 (Dashboard)** or
        - **WF-H2 (Inbox)**
        
        HH can click:
        
        > “Contact agents in my search area”
        > 
        
        HH selects:
        
        - Area (from preferences)
        - Budget
        - Buy / Rent
        - Timeline
        - Contact rules (email only / WhatsApp / phone)
        
        HH sends **one request → many agents**
        
        ➡️ Agents never see HH contact details by default.
        
        ---
        
        ## **🧑‍💼 3. AGENT FLOW (Passive → Reactive → Invited)**
        
        ### **A1 — Agent receives a request**
        
        Agent receives:
        
        - Email or WhatsApp
        - From: requests@noagent.global
        - With:
            - Area
            - Budget
            - Timeline
            - Context (“HH looking for X”)
        
        Agent can reply:
        
        - directly by email
        - or via WhatsApp
        
        ---
        
        ### **A2 — Agent reply handling**
        
        - Reply is captured by NoAgent
        - Routed to the **correct HH thread**
        - Appears in **WF-H2 (Inbox)**
        
        Agent cannot:
        
        - see HH phone
        - contact HH directly
        - start new conversations
        
        ---
        
        ### **A3 — Soft conversion to partner**
        
        Each agent reply includes:
        
        > “Replying through NoAgent helps organise requests and avoids spam.”
        > 
        
        Later (Phase 2):
        
        - Agent can claim profile
        - Become verified partner
        - Get better visibility
        
        For now:
        
        - Agents are **reactive only**
        - No login required in Phase 1
        
        ---
        
        ## **🔐 4. DATA & TRUST RULES (NON-NEGOTIABLE)**
        
        ### **Spam prevention**
        
        - No cold contact
        - No agent-initiated messages
        - No selling contact data
        - No mailing lists
        
        ### **Privacy defaults**
        
        - Email relay always on
        - WhatsApp optional
        - Phone only with HH approval
        
        ---
        
        ## **🧭 5. WHO CONTROLS WHAT (Simple Truth)**
        
        | **Actor** | **Controls** |
        | --- | --- |
        | Owner | Listing, viewings, agent involvement |
        | Home-Hunter | Preferences, contact rules, agent outreach |
        | Agent | Replies only, no initiation |
        | NoAgent | Routing, filtering, protection |

    - **Sanity-check** of the **Owner ↔ Home-Hunter ↔ Agent end-to-end flow**, focused on **correctness, gaps, edge cases, and MVP safety**. I’ll be explicit about what’s solid, what to tighten, and what to *not* overbuild now.
        
        ---
        
        ## **✅ 1. Does the flow make sense end-to-end?**
        
        **Yes — structurally it’s strong and coherent.**
        
        You have:
        
        - Clear **primary relationship**: Owner ↔ HH
        - Agents as **optional, reactive helpers**, not gatekeepers
        - NoAgent as **routing + protection layer**, not a broker
        
        That positioning is internally consistent and defensible.
        
        ---
        
        ## **🔁 2. Step-by-step sanity check (with flags)**
        
        ### **🟢 A. Owner → Listing → HH contact**
        
        ✔️ Works well
        
        - Owner lists → property ID created
        - Multiple entry points (portal, QR, WhatsApp, word of mouth)
        - HH always lands on the **correct property page**
        - Calendar logic (manual vs auto) is clear
        
        **No gaps here.**
        
        ---
        
        ### **🟢 B. HH → Book / Message → Owner**
        
        ✔️ Solid
        
        - HH gate before contact = good
        - Booking statuses are unambiguous
        - HH inbox is single source of truth
        
        **Important:**
        
        Keep **HH preferences editable at all times** (not locked after signup). You already implied this — good.
        
        ---
        
        ### **🟡 C. HH → Agents (one-to-many request)**
        
        ✔️ Conceptually right, **needs one tightening rule**
        
        What works:
        
        - HH sends **one request → many agents**
        - Agents cannot initiate
        - Responses are routed back into HH inbox
        - HH controls contact modes (email / WhatsApp / phone)
        
        **Key rule to lock (important):**
        
        > 🔒
        > 
        > 
        > **Each HH ↔ Agent request must create a unique thread ID**
        > 
        
        This ensures:
        
        - Two HHs contacting the same agent never collide
        - Replies are routed correctly
        - Filtering works cleanly
        
        ➡️ This is an **implementation note**, not a UX change.
        
        ---
        
        ### **🟡 D. Agent responses → HH**
        
        ✔️ Good, but clarify **reply surface**
        
        You have two valid options — pick **one for MVP**:
        
        **MVP-safe choice (recommended):**
        
        - Agents reply by **email or WhatsApp**
        - NoAgent relays message
        - HH replies back through NoAgent
        
        ❌ Do NOT:
        
        - Allow agents to see HH phone/email by default
        - Allow agents to add HH to their own CRM
        
        You’re right to avoid “newsletter logic” for now — that’s Phase 2.
        
        ---
        
        ### **🟢 E. Owner ↔ Agent**
        
        ✔️ Clean and optional
        
        - Owner initiates
        - Context-rich message
        - No agent spam
        
        This mirrors HH logic and keeps mental model simple.
        
        ---
        
        ## **🔐 3. Trust & anti-spam sanity check (very important)**
        
        Your rules here are **excellent** and rare in property tech:
        
        | **Risk** | **Covered?** |
        | --- | --- |
        | Agent cold-calling | ✅ blocked |
        | HH spammed by agents | ✅ blocked |
        | Owner overwhelmed | ✅ blocked |
        | Data resale | ✅ blocked |
        | Consent ambiguity | ✅ blocked |
        
        **This is a real differentiator. Keep it loud.**
        
        ---
        
        ## **🧠 4. One thing to simplify (important)**
        
        ### **❌ Don’t label agents as:**
        
        - “Available via NoAgent”
        - “Not available via NoAgent (yet)”
        
        You’re right — this adds confusion.
        
        ### **✅ Instead, use**
        
        ### **neutral framing**
        
        ### **:**
        
        - “Agents active in this area”
        - “Responds via NoAgent”
        - “New to NoAgent” (soft, positive)
        
        This avoids:
        
        - sounding like a closed marketplace
        - making HH think some agents are “worse”

    ## **🧩 WF-H1 — Home-Hunter Dashboard (Preferences)**
    
    ### **Purpose (1 sentence)**
    
    Give Home-Hunters full control over **what they’re looking for** and **how they are contacted**, while keeping agents filtered and non-intrusive.
    
    ---
    
    ## **1️⃣ Preferences Card (Always Visible on H1)**
    
    **Component:** Dashfolio Card
    
    **Location:** Top-right column (below greeting)
    
    ### **Card Title**
    
    **My Preferences**
    
    ---
    
    ### **A. Search Preferences (Required)**
    
    These define **who gets contacted** and **what matches are shown**.
    
    | **Field** | **Type** | **Notes** |
    | --- | --- | --- |
    | Looking to | Radio | Buy / Rent (single choice) |
    | Area / Postcode | Text + radius | Radius selector (5–30km) |
    | Budget range | Min–Max | Currency auto-set by country |
    | Property type | Multi-select | House, Flat, New build |
    | Bedrooms | Min | Simple numeric |
    | Timeline | Dropdown | ASAP / 3–6 months / Browsing |
    
    > 🔒 Used for **agent request context future matching**
    > 
    
    > ✨ Visible to agents **only when HH initiates contact**
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ### **B. Contact Preferences (VERY IMPORTANT)**
    
    This controls **how agents are allowed to respond**.
    
    ### **Default (pre-selected)**
    
    - ☑ **Email via NoAgent** (mandatory, cannot be disabled)
    
    ### **Optional (HH choice)**
    
    - ☐ WhatsApp (via NoAgent relay)
    - ☐ Phone calls (only after approval)
    
    ### **Safety Toggle**
    
    - ☑ **Keep my contact details private** (default ON)
    
    > Tooltip copy:
    > 
    
    > “Agents can only contact you through NoAgent unless you allow more.”
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ### **C. Agent Interaction Rules (Read-only text)**
    
    Small info block (non-editable):
    
    > No spam policy
    > 
    - Agents cannot contact you unless you ask
    - No cold calls
    - No mailing lists
    - NoAgent never sells your data
    
    (Links to About / Trust later)
    
    ---
    
    ## **2️⃣ HH Actions From WF-H1**
    
    HH can:
    
    - Edit preferences
    - Initiate **“Contact agents in my area”** (button)
    - See **summary chips**:
        - Buy / Rent
        - Area
        - Budget
    
    📌 **No agent list shown here** — discovery happens only when HH acts.
    
    ---
    
    # **🧩 WF-H2 — Inbox (Message Rules & Behaviour)**
    
    ### **Purpose:** One clean inbox for HH where **all agent replies are routed**, filtered, and controlled.
    
    ---
    
    ## **3️⃣ Inbox Structure (Locked)**
    
    **Component:** Dashfolio Table / List
    
    ### **Tabs**
    
    - **All**
    - **Agent replies**
    - **Owners**
    - **System**
    
    (No unread chaos, no folders explosion.)
    
    ---
    
    ## **4️⃣ Message Routing Rules (CRITICAL)**
    
    ### **Every HH request creates:**
    
    - One **Request ID**
    - One **isolated thread**
    - One clean conversation
    
    Even if:
    
    - HH contacted 10 agents
    - Agents reply days apart
    - Agents reply via email
    
    ➡️ Replies **never mix** between HHs or requests.
    
    ---
    
    ## **5️⃣ Message Display (Per Thread)**
    
    Each message shows:
    
    - Agent name
    - Company (if available)
    - Area covered
    - Response timestamp
    - Reply content
    
    ### **Badges**
    
    - 🟢 Responded via NoAgent
    - 🟡 External reply (email)
    - 🔒 Contact protected
    
    ---
    
    ## **6️⃣ What Agents Can & Cannot Do (Hard Rules)**
    
    ### **Agents CAN**
    
    - Reply to a HH request
    - Ask follow-up questions
    - Share listings or advice
    
    ### **Agents CANNOT**
    
    - Start conversations
    - Add HH to mailing lists
    - Call unless HH explicitly allowed
    - See HH phone number by default
    
    No exceptions in Phase 1.
    
    ---
    
    ## **7️⃣ HH Controls Inside Inbox**
    
    Per thread, HH can:
    
    - Reply
    - Mute agent
    - Close request
    - Approve phone contact (optional)
    - Ignore silently
    
    **No “unsubscribe drama”.**
    
    Ignoring = no further contact.
    
    ---
    
    ## **8️⃣ System Copy (Exact, Locked)**
    
    ### **When HH sends request**
    
    > “We’ve sent your request to selected agents. Replies will appear here.”
    > 
    
    ### **When agent replies**
    
    > “New reply from an agent covering your area.”
    > 
    
    ### **If HH has phone disabled**
    
    > “Phone contact is currently disabled. You can enable it in Preferences.”
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ## **9️⃣ Phase 2 (Design for later, NOT active)**
    
    Greyed out / placeholder only:
    
    - Agent ratings
    - Match score
    - Auto-matched listings
    - Agent performance tags
    
    ⚠️ **Do not build now.**

    - Preferences power all future logic
    
    ### **WF-H2 (Inbox)**
    
    - One inbox

- Home Hunters Agents
    
    Great — this is exactly the right moment to **lock the agent email**, because this email does a lot of strategic work for you.
    
    Below is a **clean, final Phase-1 email**, plus **explicit guidance on what the Real Agent should reply**, and **what we should / should not say**.
    
    ---
    
    # **📧 REAL AGENT EMAIL — PHASE 1 (LOCKED COPY)**
    
    ### **From**
    
    **NoAgent (yet)** <requests@noagent.global>
    
    > (The “yet” is intentional and powerful — keep it.)
    > 
    
    ### **Reply-To**
    
    reply+<thread-id>@noagent.global
    
    ---
    
    ### **Subject (critical – must scan well)**
    
    ```
    New buyer request – <AREA> (<RADIUS>) – Budget <€X–€Y> – NoAgent (yet)
    ```
    
    **Example**
    
    ```
    New buyer request – Berlin Neukölln (within 5km) – Budget €550k–€650k – NoAgent (yet)
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **Email Body (FINAL – Phase 1)**
    
    ```
    Hi <Agent Name>,
    
    A verified Home-Hunter is looking for help in your area.
    
    Looking to: Buy
    Area: Berlin Neukölln (within 5km)
    Budget: €550,000 – €650,000
    Timeline: 1–3 months
    Notes: High ceilings preferred, close to a park.
    
    You’re receiving this because you operate in this area.
    
    👉 Simply reply to this email if you’d like to help.
    Your response will be routed back to the Home-Hunter.
    
    • No cold calling
    • No mailing lists
    • Contact details are shared only if the Home-Hunter agrees
    
    — NoAgent (yet)
    A neutral platform connecting owners, home-hunters, and real agents — without commission.
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **🧠 Why this wording works**
    
    - **“NoAgent (yet)”**
        
        → signals opportunity, not exclusion
        
    - **“Verified Home-Hunter”**
        
        → increases perceived quality
        
    - **Bullet rules**
        
        → reassures agents (and protects HHs)
        
    - **“Without commission”**
        
        → VERY IMPORTANT
        
        - attracts agents
        - avoids legal / commercial confusion
        - positions you as infrastructure, not a broker
    
    ✅ You *should* say you **do not take commission**
    
    ❌ You should *not* mention pricing, portals, or future monetisation here
    
    ---
    
    # **📨 WHAT SHOULD THE REAL AGENT REPLY? (VERY IMPORTANT)**
    
    Agents must **not be confused** about what to do.
    
    ### **Instruction (implicit, not heavy-handed)**
    
    > “Simply reply to this email if you’d like to help.”
    > 
    
    That’s enough.
    
    ---
    
    ## **✅ Recommended Agent Reply Pattern (what we expect)**
    
    Agents typically reply with something like:
    
    ```
    Hi,
    
    Thanks for reaching out.
    I cover Neukölln and would be happy to help.
    
    Happy to discuss next steps or suggest suitable properties.
    Best,
    <Name>
    ```
    
    This is perfect.
    
    ---
    
    ## **🚫What agents should NOT do (but we don’t say explicitly)**
    
    They should not:
    
    - ask for phone number directly
    - add HH to a mailing list
    - CC other agents
    - send newsletters
    
    We enforce this **by system design**, not by lecturing.
    
    ---
    
    ## **🔁 How the system handles the reply**
    
    When the agent replies:
    
    1. Email hits reply+<thread-id>@noagent.global
    2. NoAgent:
        - parses it
        - attaches it to the correct HH thread
    3. HH sees in **WF-H2 Inbox**:
        - Agent name
        - Message
        - Reply button
    
    HH can then:
    
    - reply
    - ignore
    - approve phone contact
    - block agent
    
    ---
    
    - Conversation after real Agent says **“happy to help”**.
        
        
        This reply has **three jobs**:
        
        1. Confirm receipt (so the agent doesn’t resend)
        2. Set expectations (so they don’t chase)
        3. Protect the Home-Hunter (so no spam / no bypass)
        
        ---
        
        # **📧 NOAGENT → REAL AGENT (AUTO-REPLY)**
        
        **Triggered when agent replies to the request**
        
        ### **From**
        
        **NoAgent (yet)** <requests@noagent.global>
        
        ### **Subject**
        
        ```
        Thanks — we’ve shared your response with the Home-Hunter
        ```
        
        ---
        
        ## **Email Body (FINAL — Phase 1)**
        
        ```
        Hi <Agent Name>,
        
        Thanks for getting back to us.
        
        We’ve shared your response with the Home-Hunter.
        If they’d like to continue, they’ll reply here and we’ll route the conversation.
        
        For now:
        • No further action is needed
        • Please don’t contact the Home-Hunter directly
        • Contact details are shared only with their approval
        
        This helps keep requests relevant and spam-free for everyone.
        
        — NoAgent (yet)
        A neutral platform connecting owners, home-hunters, and real agents — without commission.
        ```
        
        ---
        
        ## **🧠**
        
        ## **Why this reply is important**
        
        ### **✔ It reassures the agent**
        
        - “My reply didn’t disappear”
        - “I’m not expected to chase”
        
        ### **✔ It sets boundaries (politely)**
        
        - No direct contact
        - No follow-ups
        - No pressure
        
        ### **✔ It protects the Home-Hunter**
        
        - Prevents phone calls “just checking”
        - Prevents off-platform outreach
        
        ### **✔ It keeps NoAgent neutral**
        
        - You’re not selling
        - You’re not brokering
        - You’re coordinating
        
        ---
        
        ## **🔒**
        
        ## **Behaviour locked by this reply**
        
        - Agents **wait** instead of chasing
        - HH responds only if interested
        - NoAgent controls the next step
        - No escalation unless HH opts in
        
        This is critical to prevent the **classic agent behaviour**:
        
        > “Just following up…”
        > 
        
        > “Wanted to check if you saw my email…”
        > 
        
        That never happens here.
        
        ---
        
        ## **🔁**
        
        ## **What happens next (system behaviour)**
        
        1. Agent reply → captured
        2. HH sees it in **WF-H2 Inbox**
        3. HH can:
            - reply
            - ignore
            - approve phone contact
            - block agent
        4. If HH replies → conversation continues via NoAgent relay
        
        No extra emails are sent unless HH acts.
        
        ---
        
        ## **🚫**
        
        ## **What we deliberately do NOT include**
        
        We do **not**:
        
        - ask the agent to sign up
        - promote features
        - mention dashboards
        - mention portals
        - mention pricing
        
        Trust first. Conversion later.
        
        ---
        
        ## **✅**
        
        ## **FINAL LOCK**
        
        - ✔ Auto-reply is sent **once**
        - ✔ Tone is calm, neutral, respectful
        - ✔ No call-to-action beyond “wait”
        - ✔ Aligns perfectly with your no-spam promise
        
        ---
        
        ### **If you want next:**
        
        I can now:
        
        - write the **HH-facing notification copy** (“Agent X replied…”)
        - or produce the **WhatsApp equivalents** of all three messages
        - or convert these into **SendGrid / Resend templates**
        
        You’ve now fully closed the **Owner ↔ HH ↔ Agent communication loop**.

    - ✅ Say **“without commission”**
    - ✅ Keep reply action dead simple
    - ✅ Do not force signup
    - ✅ Do not expose HH contact details
    - ✅ Use email as a *relay*, not a mailbox
    
    ---
    
    ## **Next logical step (if you want)**
    
    We can now:
    
    1. Write the **HH-facing inbox copy** for agent replies
    2. Write the **Owner-facing version** of this same email
    3. Convert this into **SendGrid / Resend template JSON**
    4. Or lock **WhatsApp version** of the same message
    
    Just tell me where to go next.

- **The Communication Model (Hybrid, Intentional)**
    
    ---
    
    ## **Core principle (lock this)**
    
    > NoAgent is the system of record.
    > 
    
    > Email and WhatsApp are delivery channels — not the source of truth.
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ## **1️⃣ What happens by default (Phase 1)**
    
    ### **Inside the platform (primary)**
    
    - Inquiries
    - Viewing requests
    - Offers / applications
    - Status changes
    
    ➡️ All **stored and visible** in:
    
    - **WF-O3 — Inquiries & Offers**
    - **WF-H2 — Inbox**
    
    ---
    
    ### **Email (secondary, bridged)**
    
    Email is used for:
    
    - Notifications
    - Replies that deep-link back into NoAgent
    
    **But**:
    
    - Emails never become the “only place” a conversation exists
    - Every email contains a **link back** to the platform
    
    ---
    
    ## **2️⃣ Owner ↔ Home-Hunter: how email actually works**
    
    ### **Scenario A — HH sends inquiry via NoAgent (web)**
    
    - Message stored in NoAgent
    - Owner receives **email notification**
    - Email contains:
        
        > “Reply in NoAgent” button
        > 
    
    ➡️ Clicking opens WF-O3 conversation view
    
    ---
    
    ### **Scenario B — Owner replies**
    
    ### **from email**
    
    This is important.
    
    **Two safe options (Phase 1 MVP choice):**
    
    ### **Option 1 (Simplest, recommended MVP)**
    
    - Email reply **redirects to platform**
    - No email-to-email threading
    
    Email footer copy:
    
    > “To reply, open this conversation in NoAgent.”
    > 
    
    ✔️ Zero parsing complexity
    
    ✔️ No data loss
    
    ✔️ Clean UX
    
    ### **Option 2 (Phase 2)**
    
    - Email replies are parsed and synced back into NoAgent
    - Requires:
        - Reply-to tokens
        - Inbound email parsing (SendGrid / Postmark)
    
    We **do not need this for MVP**.
    
    ---
    
    ## **3️⃣ WhatsApp (explicitly treated as an external channel)**
    
    WhatsApp is:
    
    - Allowed
    - Logged
    - Not forced
    
    ### **How it works**
    
    - WF-O5 CTA: “Message on WhatsApp”
    - Opens WhatsApp with prefilled message + link
    - System logs:
        - source = whatsapp
        - timestamp
        - placeId
    - Actual chat happens in WhatsApp
    
    ✔️ Mirrors real behaviour
    
    ✔️ Owners are comfortable
    
    ✔️ No illusion of control
    
    ---
    
    ## **4️⃣ What we deliberately do NOT do**
    
    ❌ No exposing owner’s private email publicly
    
    ❌ No unmanaged email threads
    
    ❌ No “reply anywhere, we’ll figure it out” chaos
    
    ❌ No pretending WhatsApp is “in-app chat”
    
    This keeps trust high and scope sane.
    
    ---
    
    ## **5️⃣ Summary Table — Communication Channels**
    
    | **Channel** | **Used?** | **Stored in NoAgent** | **Purpose** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | In-app messaging | ✅ | ✅ Yes | Primary record |
    | Email notifications | ✅ | ✅ Metadata only | Alerts + deep links |
    | Email replies | ⚠️ Phase 2 | Optional | Advanced sync |
    | WhatsApp | ✅ | ⚠️ Logged only | Fast external chat |
    | SMS | ✅ | ⚠️ Logged only | Resolver + alerts |
    | Phone calls | ✅ | ⚠️ Logged only | Discovery |
    
    ---
    
    ## **6️⃣ What the user experiences (important)**
    
    ### **Owner**
    
    - “I get emails, but everything important lives in NoAgent.”
    - “I can still use WhatsApp if I want.”
    
    ### **Home-Hunter**
    
    - “I can message and book easily.”
    - “I’m never forced to use a weird chat system.”
    
    ---
    
    ## **7️⃣ What to tell the designer (one paragraph, copy-paste)**
    
    > Communication is platform-first.
    > 
    
    > Messages, bookings, and offers are managed inside NoAgent.
    > 
    
    > Email and WhatsApp are supported as notification and external channels, always linking back to the listing or conversation.
    > 
    
    > NoAgent remains the system of record at all times.
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ## **🔒 FINAL LOCK — Email & Messaging**
    
    > NoAgent integrates email for notifications and deep-linked replies, while keeping all critical communication inside the platform.
    > 
    
    > External channels (WhatsApp, SMS, phone) are supported and logged, but do not replace NoAgent as the system of record.
    > 
    
    ---
    
    If you want, next we can:
    
    - lock **exact email templates** (Owner + HH), or
    - specify **WF-O3 UI labels** (“Email”, “WhatsApp”, “Portal”), or
    - decide **when to add email-reply syncing (Phase 2)**.
    
    Just say the word.
    
- **Email Templates (Phase 1)**
    
    Perfect — below are **exact, copy-paste-ready email templates** for **Phase 1**, written to:
    
    - keep **NoAgent as the system of record**
    - avoid messy email threads
    - push users back into the platform
    - work globally (country / currency agnostic)
    - be automation-safe (SendGrid / Postmark / SES)
    
    I’ve grouped them by **trigger**, with **subject, body, CTA, and logic notes**.
    
    ---
    
    ## **TEMPLATE 1 — New Inquiry Received (Owner)**
    
    **Trigger**
    
    Home-Hunter sends an inquiry via WF-O5 or WF-H flow.
    
    **To**
    
    Owner email
    
    ### **Subject**
    
    ```
    New inquiry for your listing on NoAgent
    ```
    
    ### **Body**
    
    ```
    Hi {{owner_first_name}},
    
    You’ve received a new inquiry for your listing:
    
    {{property_title}}
    {{property_address}}
    
    From:
    {{hh_first_name}} {{hh_last_name}}
    {{hh_status_badge}}
    (e.g. Verified · Cash Buyer / Mortgage in Principle / Renting)
    
    Message:
    “{{inquiry_message}}”
    
    You can reply, schedule a viewing, or review the profile directly in NoAgent.
    
    [ View inquiry & reply ]
    
    —
    NoAgent
    No fees. No commission.
    ```
    
    ### **CTA**
    
    **View inquiry & reply** → deep link to
    
    /owner/inquiries/{{conversation_id}}
    
    ### **Notes**
    
    - ❌ Do NOT allow reply-by-email in Phase 1
    - ✔ Button is the only reply path
    - ✔ Status badge builds trust immediately
    
    ---
    
    ## **TEMPLATE 2 — Viewing Booked (Owner)**
    
    **Trigger**
    
    HH books a viewing via WF-O4 calendar.
    
    **To**

    ```

    ```
    
    ### **Body**
    
    ```

    {{property_title}}
    {{property_address}}
    
    When:
    {{viewing_date}}
    {{viewing_time}}
    {{timezone}}

    {{hh_first_name}} {{hh_last_name}}
    {{hh_status_badge}}

    [ View calendar & details ]
    
    —
    NoAgent
    ```
    
    ### **CTA**
    
    **View calendar & details** →
    
    /owner/calendar?event={{event_id}}
    
    ### **Notes**
    
    - Google Calendar sync already happened
    - Email is confirmation + backup
    
    ---

    ---
    
    # **🔒 FINAL LOCK — Email Strategy**
    
    > Emails are used for notifications and confirmations only.
    > 
    
    > All actions and replies are deep-linked back into NoAgent.
    > 
    
    > No unmanaged email threads exist in Phase 1.
    > 
    
    ---
    
- **SMS & WhatsApp templates**
    - **short** (SMS-safe)
    - **link-driven** (system of record stays NoAgent)
    - **globally usable**
    - **Twilio / WhatsApp Business–ready**
    
    ---
    
    # **📱 NoAgent — SMS Templates (Phase 1)**
    
    ## **SMS-1 — After Phone Call (Resolver Start)**
    
    **Trigger**
    
    Inbound call to generic portal number (missed or answered)
    
    **To**
    
    Home-Hunter phone number
    
    **Message**
    
    ```
    Thanks for calling about a NoAgent listing.
    Reply with the postcode or street + number to get the booking link.
    ```
    
    **Notes**
    
    - No links yet (avoid confusion)
    - Works globally
    - Sets clear next action
    
    ---
    
    ## **SMS-2 — Resolver Success (Single Match)**
    
    **Trigger**
    
    HH replies with address/postcode → 1 match found
    
    **Message**
    
    ```
    Got it! Here’s the listing and live availability:
    https://noagent.global/p/{{place_id}}
    ```
    
    **Notes**
    
    - Primary conversion moment
    - Link always resolves correctly
    
    ---
    
    ## **SMS-3 — Resolver Disambiguation (Multiple Matches)**
    
    **Trigger**
    
    Address matches more than one listing
    
    **Message**
    
    ```
    We found multiple listings:
    1) {{short_address_1}}
    2) {{short_address_2}}
    
    Reply 1 or 2 to continue.
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **SMS-4 — Resolver Failure (No Match)**
    
    **Trigger**
    
    Address cannot be resolved
    
    **Message**
    
    ```
    Sorry — we couldn’t find that listing.
    Please reply with postcode and house number.
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **SMS-5 — Viewing Request Acknowledgement (No Slots)**
    
    **Trigger**
    
    HH requests viewing but no slots available
    
    **Message**
    
    ```
    Your viewing request was sent.
    The owner will be notified and may add availability soon.
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **SMS-6 — Viewing Confirmation (Optional)**
    
    **Trigger**
    
    Viewing booked successfully (optional backup to email)
    
    **Message**
    
    ```
    Viewing confirmed for {{short_address}} on {{date}} at {{time}}.
    Details: https://noagent.global/p/{{place_id}}
    ```
    
    ---
    
    # **💬 NoAgent — WhatsApp Templates (Phase 1)**
    
    > WhatsApp is treated as an
    > 
    > 
    > **external but logged channel**
    > 
    
    > Messages open WhatsApp with
    > 
    > 
    > **pre-filled text**
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ## **WA-1 — “Message Owner” CTA (Prefill)**
    
    **Trigger**
    
    HH clicks “Message on WhatsApp” on WF-O5
    
    **Prefilled Message**
    
    ```
    Hi, I’m interested in this property:
    https://noagent.global/p/{{place_id}}
    ```
    
    **Notes**
    
    - No friction
    - Link anchors identity
    - Owner instantly knows which property
    
    ---
    
    ## **WA-2 — After Call Follow-Up (Optional Alternative to SMS)**
    
    **Trigger**
    
    HH calls and WhatsApp is available
    
    **Message**
    
    ```
    Thanks for your interest in a NoAgent listing.
    View details and book a viewing here:
    https://noagent.global/p/{{place_id}}
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **WA-3 — Owner-Initiated Follow-Up (Manual)**
    
    **Trigger**
    
    Owner chooses to contact HH via WhatsApp
    
    **Suggested Copy**
    
    ```
    Hi {{hh_first_name}}, thanks for your interest.
    You can view availability and manage your booking here:
    https://noagent.global/p/{{place_id}}
    ```
    
    ---
    
    # **🔗 Link Rules (LOCKED)**
    
    All SMS / WhatsApp links must:
    
    - resolve to **Place ID**
    - never expose internal IDs explicitly
    - support ?src= tags optionally
    
    Example:
    
    ```
    /p/{{place_id}}?src=call-sms
    /p/{{place_id}}?src=whatsapp
    ```

    | **Template** | **Used In** |
    | --- | --- |
    | SMS-1 → SMS-4 | Portal calls → WF-O5 |
    | SMS-5 | WF-O5 (no slots flow) |
    | SMS-6 | WF-H1 / WF-O4 |
    | WA-1 | WF-O5 |
    | WA-2 | Call follow-up |
    | WA-3 | WF-O3 (Owner action) |

    # **🔌 External Services Required**
    
    | **Service** | **Purpose** |
    | --- | --- |
    | **Twilio SMS** | Resolver + confirmations |
    | **Twilio Voice** | Call capture |
    | **WhatsApp Business API** | Messaging |
    | **Link shortener (optional)** | SMS optimisation |
    
    ---
    
    # **🔒 FINAL LOCK — SMS & WhatsApp**
    
    > SMS is used for automated resolution and confirmations.
    > 
    
    > WhatsApp is supported as a fast external channel with pre-filled, Place-ID-linked messages.
    > 
    
    > All communication paths lead back to the canonical Public Property Page.
    > 
    
    ---
    
- **Twilio Number Strategy (Per Country)**
    
    Designed to:
    
    - keep costs predictable
    - minimise operational complexity
    - support **call → SMS resolver**, WhatsApp, and notifications
    - scale cleanly country by country
    
    This is **locked and handover-ready** for Product, Dev, and Ops.
    
    ---
    
    - **Twilio webhook logic** (events + payloads)
        
        **Phase-1 Twilio webhook spec** you can hand straight to a developer. It covers:
        
        - **Voice call capture**
        - **SMS resolver (2-way)**
        - **Optional WhatsApp inbound/outbound hooks**
        - **Event names + payload shapes**
        - **State machine + matching logic**
        - **Security + idempotency**
        
        ---
        
        ## **0) Overview (what we’re building)**
        
        We support **generic portal numbers** per country. When a Home-Hunter calls, we:
        
        1. forward the call (optional), and
        2. auto-SMS a resolver prompt, and
        3. parse their SMS reply to identify the **Place ID**, then
        4. send the correct **/p/{placeId}** link.
        
        Everything logs to NoAgent as events.
        
        ---
        
        # **1) Twilio Webhooks You Need**
        
        ## **A) Voice: Incoming Call Webhook**
        
        **Twilio** → POST /webhooks/twilio/voice/incoming
        
        **Used for**
        
        - Detect inbound call
        - Determine which tracking number was called
        - Start resolver session
        - Return TwiML to forward call and/or play message
        
        ---
        
        ## **B) Voice: Call Status Callback**
        
        **Twilio** → POST /webhooks/twilio/voice/status
        
        **Used for**
        
        - call completed / no-answer / busy
        - analytics + debugging
        
        ---
        
        ## **C) SMS: Incoming Message Webhook**
        
        **Twilio** → POST /webhooks/twilio/sms/incoming
        
        **Used for**
        
        - Resolver replies (postcode/address)
        - Disambiguation replies (1/2/3)
        - Generic inbound texts
        
        ---
        
        ## **D) SMS: Delivery Status Callback (Optional but recommended)**
        
        **Twilio** → POST /webhooks/twilio/sms/status
        
        **Used for**
        
        - mark SMS delivered/failed
        - alert Integrations dashboard
        
        ---
        
        ## **E) WhatsApp: Incoming Message Webhook (Optional Phase 1)**
        
        **Twilio** → POST /webhooks/twilio/whatsapp/incoming
        
        **Used for**
        
        - log inbound WhatsApp messages
        - auto-reply with listing link if resolvable (optional)
        
        > You can ship Phase 1 without inbound WhatsApp parsing, but this keeps the door open.
        > 
        
        ---
        
        # **2) Data You Store (minimal schema)**
        
        ## **ResolverSession (core)**
        
        Created on inbound call, updated on SMS replies.
        
        ```
        ResolverSession {
          "id": "rsn_123",
          "country": "UK",
          "channel": "voice_sms",
          "fromPhone": "+447700900123",
          "toPhone": "+442039999999",          // Twilio number they called
          "portal": "rightmove",               // derived from toPhone mapping
          "status": "awaiting_input",          // awaiting_input | awaiting_choice | resolved | failed | expired
          "candidates": [
            {"placeId":"place_8f3a92c1","label":"12 Park Rd (2 bed)"},
            {"placeId":"place_9aa7710b","label":"12 Park Rd (1 bed)"}
          ],
          "resolvedPlaceId": null,
          "attemptCount": 0,
          "lastMessageAt": "2026-01-01T10:00:00Z",
          "expiresAt": "2026-01-01T10:30:00Z",
          "twilio": {
            "callSid": "CAxxx",
            "lastInboundSmsSid": "SMxxx",
            "lastOutboundSmsSid": "SMyyy"
          }
        }
        ```
        
        ## **PhoneNumberRouting (config)**
        
        Maps each country number to portal/campaign.
        
        ```
        PhoneNumberRouting {
          "toPhone": "+442039999999",
          "country": "UK",
          "label": "UK-Rightmove",
          "portal": "rightmove",
          "forwardTo": "+447911111111"  // optional
        }
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **3) Event Names (for analytics + admin)**
        
        All events must include: placeId (if known), source, country, timestamp.
        
        | **Event** | **When** |
        | --- | --- |
        | call_received | inbound voice hit |
        | call_forwarded | forwarded initiated |
        | sms_sent | outbound SMS queued |
        | sms_delivered | status callback delivered |
        | resolver_started | session created |
        | resolver_input_received | SMS reply received |
        | resolver_candidates_returned | ambiguity menu sent |
        | resolver_resolved | placeId resolved + link sent |
        | resolver_failed | could not resolve |
        | whatsapp_inbound_received | WA message logged |
        
        ---
        
        # **4) Webhook Payloads (Twilio → NoAgent)**
        
        ## **A) Voice Incoming:**
        
        ## **/voice/incoming**
        
        Twilio will send form-encoded fields. Parse at least:
        
        ```
        {
          "CallSid": "CAxxxxxxxx",
          "From": "+447700900123",
          "To": "+442039999999",
          "Called": "+442039999999",
          "Direction": "inbound",
          "CallerCountry": "GB",
          "CallStatus": "ringing"
        }
        ```
        
        ### **Your server must respond with**
        
        ### **TwiML**
        
        **Option A (recommended): forward call + start SMS resolver**
        
        ```
        <Response>
          <Dial timeout="20">{{forwardTo}}</Dial>
        </Response>
        ```
        
        **Option B: if no forwardTo exists, play message**
        
        ```
        <Response>
          <Say>Thanks for calling NoAgent. You'll receive a text message with a booking link.</Say>
        </Response>
        ```
        
        ### **Server side actions on incoming call**
        
        1. Lookup routing by To
        2. Create ResolverSession
        3. Fire call_received, resolver_started
        4. Send SMS-1 prompt (see below)
        
        ---
        
        ## **B) Voice Status:**
        
        ## **/voice/status**
        
        Minimum parse:
        
        ```
        {
          "CallSid": "CAxxxxxxxx",
          "CallStatus": "completed|no-answer|busy|failed",
          "From": "+447700900123",
          "To": "+442039999999",
          "CallDuration": "42"
        }
        ```
        
        Store for diagnostics + analytics.
        
        ---
        
        ## **C) SMS Incoming:**
        
        ## **/sms/incoming**
        
        Parse:
        
        ```
        {
          "MessageSid": "SMxxxxxxxx",
          "From": "+447700900123",
          "To": "+442039999999",
          "Body": "E8 3JP",
          "NumMedia": "0"
        }
        ```
        
        ### **Server side algorithm**
        
        1. Find active ResolverSession by:
            - fromPhone + toPhone where status in (awaiting_input, awaiting_choice)
            - newest session, not expired
        2. If none: create a “cold” session and ask for postcode/address (optional)
        3. If awaiting_input:
            - Normalize input (trim, uppercase, collapse spaces)
            - Try resolve to Place candidates (see matching)
        4. If awaiting_choice:
            - Expect 1..n
            - Resolve to selected placeId
        5. Send outbound SMS accordingly
        
        ---
        
        ## **D) SMS Status:**
        
        ## **/sms/status**
        
        ## **(optional)**
        
        Parse:
        
        ```
        {
          "MessageSid": "SMoutbound",
          "MessageStatus": "delivered|failed|undelivered",
          "To": "+447700900123",
          "From": "+442039999999"
        }
        ```
        
        Update Integrations (WF-A4) and session log.
        
        ---
        
        ## **E) WhatsApp Incoming:**
        
        ## **/whatsapp/incoming**
        
        ## **(optional)**
        
        Twilio uses From=whatsapp:+44... style.
        
        ```
        {
          "MessageSid": "SMwa...",
          "From": "whatsapp:+447700900123",
          "To": "whatsapp:+4420XXXXXXX",
          "Body": "Hi, I'm interested..."
        }
        ```
        
        Phase 1: log only
        
        Phase 2: attempt to detect /p/{placeId} link and auto-route.
        
        ---
        
        # **5) Resolver Matching Logic (Phase 1)**
        
        ## **Input types accepted**
        
        1. Postcode/ZIP (best)
        2. Street + number
        3. Portal URL pasted
        4. “12 Park Rd” without postcode (fuzzy)
        
        ## **Matching steps**
        
        1. If input contains noagent.global/p/ → extract placeId immediately
        2. If UK postcode pattern → query listings by postcode in active/draft/live
        3. If contains digits + street tokens → fuzzy search by normalized address fields
        4. Apply confidence scoring:
            - exact postcode + house number = high
            - street + number = medium
            - street only = low (return candidates)
        
        ## **Outcome rules**
        
        - **1 high-confidence match** → resolved
        - **2–5 matches** → send disambiguation menu
        - **0 matches** → ask for postcode + house number
        
        ---
        
        # **6) Outbound Messages (the exact automated wording)**
        
        ## **SMS-1 Prompt (after call)**
        
        ```
        Thanks for calling about a NoAgent listing.
        Reply with the postcode or street + number to get the booking link.
        ```
        
        ## **SMS-2 Success**
        
        ```
        Got it! Here’s the listing and live availability:
        https://noagent.global/p/{{placeId}}?src={{portal}}-call
        ```
        
        ## **SMS-3 Disambiguation**
        
        ```
        We found multiple listings:
        1) {{label1}}
        2) {{label2}}
        Reply 1 or 2 to continue.
        ```
        
        ## **SMS-4 No match**
        
        ```
        Sorry — we couldn’t find that listing.
        Please reply with postcode and house number.
        ```
        
        ---
        
        # **7) Security & Reliability (must-haves)**
        
        ## **Validate Twilio signatures**
        
        - Verify X-Twilio-Signature for each webhook
        - Reject invalid signatures (401)
        
        ## **Idempotency**
        
        - Store processed CallSid and MessageSid
        - If received twice, return 200 without re-sending SMS
        
        ## **Rate limiting**
        
        - Per From number, max N messages per minute
        
        ## **Session expiry**
        
        - Expire ResolverSession after **30 minutes**
        - If expired, restart with SMS-1 prompt
        
        ---
        
        # **8) Admin Surfacing (WF-A4 Integration Overview)**
        
        At minimum display per country:
        
        - Voice status (Active/Degraded)
        - SMS status (Active/Degraded)
        - Last inbound call time
        - Last SMS sent time
        - Last delivery status
        - Running cost placeholder
        
        ---
        
        # **✅ Build Checklist (Developer)**
        
        1. Create Twilio number mapping table (country/portal → To number)
        2. Implement /voice/incoming TwiML responder + ResolverSession creation
        3. Implement /sms/incoming resolver state machine
        4. Implement outbound SMS sending with templated text
        5. Implement signature verification + idempotency
        6. Log events to analytics store with placeId when known
        7. Expose basic status to WF-A4
        
        ---
        
         
        
    - **Responsibility Split**
        
        ---
        
        ### **Twilio = Pipes & Triggers**
        
        Twilio is responsible for:
        
        - Phone numbers (per country)
        - Receiving calls
        - Receiving SMS / WhatsApp messages
        - Sending SMS / WhatsApp messages
        - Forwarding calls
        - Calling your webhooks
        
        👉 Twilio does **not** understand properties, users, bookings, or Place IDs.
        
        ---
        
        ### **NoAgent = Brain & System of Record**
        
        NoAgent is responsible for:
        
        - Creating Place IDs
        - Resolver logic (postcode → property)
        - Session state (“awaiting reply”, “resolved”, etc.)
        - Business rules
        - Analytics
        - Admin visibility
        - Security decisions
        - UX outcomes (which page to send)
        
        👉 Twilio never decides *what* to send — only *delivers* it.
        
        ---
        
        ## **📍 Where “they sit” technically**
        
        ### **1️⃣ Twilio Console (Configuration only)**
        
        In Twilio you configure:
        
        - Phone numbers
        - WhatsApp sender
        - Webhook URLs
        
        Example (UK number):
        
        | **Setting** | **Value** |
        | --- | --- |
        | Voice webhook | POST https://api.noagent.global/webhooks/twilio/voice/incoming |
        | Voice status callback | POST https://api.noagent.global/webhooks/twilio/voice/status |
        | SMS webhook | POST https://api.noagent.global/webhooks/twilio/sms/incoming |
        | SMS status callback | POST https://api.noagent.global/webhooks/twilio/sms/status |
        | WhatsApp webhook | POST https://api.noagent.global/webhooks/twilio/whatsapp/incoming |
        
        That’s **all** Twilio needs to know.
        
        ---
        
        ### **2️⃣ NoAgent Backend (where the real work happens)**
        
        Inside NoAgent you implement:
        
        - /webhooks/twilio/* endpoints
        - ResolverSession state machine
        - Place ID matching
        - Message templates
        - Event logging
        - Admin dashboards (WF-A4)
        
        Twilio just calls your URLs.
        
        ---
        
        ## **🧠 Mental Model (very important)**
        
        > Twilio is a dumb courier.
        > 
        
        > NoAgent is the control tower.
        > 
        
        If you ever switch from Twilio to another provider:
        
        - 90% of your logic stays untouched
        - Only webhook adapters change
        
        That’s exactly how you want it architected.
        
        ---
        
        ## **❌ What does not sit in Twilio**
        
        - Place IDs
        - Property matching
        - “Which property is this?” logic
        - Disambiguation menus
        - Booking links
        - Business rules
        - Analytics
        - Admin monitoring
        
        Those all sit **inside NoAgent**.
        
        ---
        
        ## **🧩 How this shows up in Admin (WF-A4)**
        
        Admin sees:
        
        - “Twilio (UK)” — Active / Degraded
        - Last inbound call
        - Last SMS sent
        - Cost estimate
        
        But **no business logic is editable there**.
        
        ---
        
        ## **🔒 FINAL LOCK STATEMENT**
        
        > Twilio is used purely as the communications infrastructure (voice, SMS, WhatsApp).
        > 
        
        > All workflows, state, and property resolution logic live inside NoAgent.
        > 
        
        > Twilio triggers webhooks; NoAgent decides what happens.
        > 
        
        ---
        
    - **Communications Without Twilio (Fallback Strategy)**
        
        Got it. Here’s a **clean fallback plan** that preserves the **same product behaviour** (call → identify property → send booking link) even if Twilio is unavailable or blocked in a country.
        
        I’ll lay it out as **3 fallback tiers**, from easiest to strongest.
        
        ---
        
        ## **Core principle (unchanged)**
        
        > NoAgent remains the brain + system of record.
        > 
        
        > Fallback providers are just transport.
        > 
        
        So the Place ID / resolver logic stays identical; only the “pipes” change.
        
        ---
        
        # **Tier 1 — “No Phone Automation” (MVP fallback, zero infra)**
        
        ### **What works**
        
        - Portal click-through links → WF-O5 booking ✅
        - QR codes on signboard → WF-O5 booking ✅
        - WhatsApp click-to-chat links → WF-O5 booking ✅
        - Email auto-replies (portal email leads) ✅
        
        ### **What you lose**
        
        - Automated call → SMS resolver ❌
        
        ### **How you handle calls**
        
        - Calls go to:
            - the Owner’s own number, or
            - a manual support number (mobile)
        
        Then you use **human-in-the-loop**:
        
        **Manual script (owner/support says):**
        
        > “Can you open noagent.global and search the postcode, or scan the QR on the sign? You can book online instantly.”
        > 
        
        ✅ This is acceptable early on if most conversions come from portal links + QR.
        
        ---
        
        # **Tier 2 — Replace Twilio with “Telephony + SMS Alternative”**
        
        You keep the **same exact webhooks + resolver logic**, but swap provider.
        
        ## **Options (depending on country)**
        
        - **Vonage (Nexmo)**: SMS + Voice APIs (closest to Twilio model)
        - **MessageBird**: SMS + Voice (good EU coverage)
        - **Infobip**: strong international telecom coverage
        - **Plivo / Telnyx**: often cheaper, similar primitives
        
        ### **How it works (same architecture)**
        
        - Provider receives call/SMS
        - Provider hits your webhook endpoints
        - NoAgent creates ResolverSession
        - NoAgent sends SMS with /p/{placeId} link
        
        ✅ Behaviour identical
        
        ✅ Minimal code changes (adapter layer only)
        
        ✅ Still country-by-country numbers
        
        **Developer note:** implement a CommsProvider interface:
        
        - send_sms()
        - forward_call()
        - verify_signature()
        - parse_inbound()
        
        Then Twilio/Vonage/MessageBird are plugins.
        
        ---
        
        # **Tier 3 — “No SMS Provider”: Web-based Resolver Link (Strongest non-SMS fallback)**
        
        If SMS APIs are hard in a country, do this:
        
        ### **Use a “Call Landing URL” instead of SMS**
        
        You publish a **short, human-friendly URL** everywhere you would have used a phone flow:
        
        - On portals (in description / media)
        - On signs
        - In printed material
        
        Example:
        
        ```
        noagent.global/visit
        ```
        
        When someone arrives, show a simple resolver page:
        
        ### **WF-H0 — “Find the listing” (tiny page)**
        
        - Input: postcode / address
        - Optional: “Paste portal link”
        - Button: “Find availability”
        - Result: takes them to WF-O5
        
        This replaces “reply by SMS” with “enter on web”.
        
        ✅ No SMS dependency
        
        ✅ Works globally
        
        ✅ Keeps conversion online
        
        ⚠️ Slightly more friction than SMS
        
        ---
        
        # **Fallback WhatsApp Without Twilio**
        
        Even without Twilio you can support WhatsApp as a **click-to-chat link**:
        
        - Use a WhatsApp Business number (or even regular initially)
        - Public CTA opens:
        
        ```
        https://wa.me/<number>?text=<prefilled>
        ```
        
        Prefilled text includes:
        
        ```
        https://noagent.global/p/{placeId}
        ```
        
        ✅ Works without WhatsApp API
        
        ⚠️ You won’t have inbound webhooks/logging (Phase 1 acceptable)
        
        ---
        
        # **Fallback Email Without Twilio (recommended regardless)**
        
        Email is independent:
        
        - **Postmark / SendGrid / SES**
        - Triggers:
            - inquiry notifications
            - viewing confirmations
            - portal email auto-replies (if you ingest those leads)
        
        ---
        
        # **What changes in the product (UX)**
        
        ## **If Twilio (or equivalent) is active**
        
        - Call → auto SMS resolver → direct listing link
        
        ## **If Twilio is down / not available (country toggle)**
        
        - Calls become manual
        - Stronger push to:
            - QR codes
            - portal click links
            - website “Find listing” flow
        
        ### **Microcopy to support fallback (one-liner)**
        
        On WF-O5 / footer / support:
        
        > “Prefer to book online? View live availability on this page.”
        > 
        
        ---
        
        # **Admin control (WF-A4 Integrations)**
        
        Add a country toggle:
        
        | **Country** | **Voice/SMS mode** |
        | --- | --- |
        | UK | Provider mode (Twilio/Vonage/etc) |
        | DE | Web-only fallback |
        
        Status displayed:
        
        - “Automation: Active” or “Web-only fallback”
        
        ---
        
        # **🔒 FINAL LOCK — Without Twilio**
        
        > NoAgent can operate without Twilio by relying on portal click-through links, QR codes, WhatsApp click-to-chat, and email.
        > 
        
        > For call-based flows, NoAgent either uses a compatible telecom provider (Vonage/MessageBird/etc.) with the same webhook architecture, or falls back to a web-based listing resolver page.
        > 
        
        > Place ID logic remains unchanged in all cases.
        > 
        
        ---
        
    
    # **Core principle (lock this)**
    
    > Numbers are allocated per country and per channel, not per property.
    > 
    
    > Property resolution happens via
    > 
    > 
    > **Place ID**
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ## **1️⃣ Minimum Numbers Required per Country (Phase 1)**
    
    ### **Baseline (MVP)**
    
    For each country you operate in, you need:
    
    | **Channel** | **Purpose** | **Numbers per Country** |
    | --- | --- | --- |
    | Voice (Calls) | Portal calls, signboards | **1** |
    | SMS | Resolver, confirmations | **1** |
    | WhatsApp | Messaging | **1** |
    | **Total** |  | **2–3 numbers** |
    
    > In most countries,
    > 
    > 
    > **one Twilio number can handle BOTH Voice + SMS**
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ## **2️⃣ Recommended Setup by Country (Phase 1)**
    
    ### **🇬🇧 United Kingdom**
    
    | **Item** | **Recommendation** |
    | --- | --- |
    | Number type | Local UK number |
    | Voice | Yes (call capture + forward) |
    | SMS | Yes (resolver + confirmations) |
    | WhatsApp | Yes (Business API) |
    | Count | **1 UK number** (voice + SMS) + **1 WhatsApp sender** |
    
    ---
    
    ### **🇩🇪 Germany**
    
    | **Item** | **Recommendation** |
    | --- | --- |
    | Number type | Local German number |
    | Voice | Optional (less call-heavy market) |
    | SMS | Yes |
    | WhatsApp | Yes (very high adoption) |
    | Count | **1 DE number** (SMS, optional voice) + **1 WhatsApp sender** |
    
    ---
    
    ### **🇪🇺 EU (Other Countries – Phase 2)**
    
    | **Item** | **Recommendation** |
    | --- | --- |
    | Number type | Local if available, otherwise EU |
    | Voice | Optional |
    | SMS | Yes |
    | WhatsApp | Yes |
    | Count | **1 number per country** |
    
    ---
    
    ## **3️⃣ Number Purpose Matrix (What each number does)**
    
    | **Number** | **Handles** | **Example Use** |
    | --- | --- | --- |
    | Country Voice/SMS | Calls + SMS | Rightmove call → SMS resolver |
    | WhatsApp Sender | WhatsApp messages | “Message on WhatsApp” CTA |
    | (Optional) Toll-free | Support | Admin / later phase |
    
    ---
    
    ## **4️⃣ Call Flow (Generic Number, Property-Safe)**
    
    **Inbound call → Country number**
    
    1. Call comes in
    2. Forward call to:
        - Owner (optional)
        - Central support line
    3. Auto-SMS sent:
        
        > “Reply with postcode or street + number to get the booking link.”
        > 
    4. Reply resolves to **Place ID**
    5. SMS back with:
    
    ```
    https://noagent.global/p/{placeId}
    ```
    
    ✅ No property-specific numbers
    
    ✅ No confusion
    
    ✅ Works across portals
    
    ---
    
    ## **5️⃣ WhatsApp Strategy (Important)**
    
    - WhatsApp uses **Business API**
    - One sender per country is enough
    - Messages are **prefilled with Place ID link**
    - Chats live in WhatsApp, not mirrored
    
    Example prefill:
    
    ```
    Hi, I’m interested in this property:
    https://noagent.global/p/{placeId}
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **6️⃣ Cost Expectations (Very Rough, Phase 1)**
    
    > These are
    > 
    > 
    > **order-of-magnitude**
    > 
    
    | **Item** | **Monthly (per country)** |
    | --- | --- |
    | Phone number | €1–€5 |
    | SMS (resolver + confirms) | €10–€30 |
    | WhatsApp | Usage-based (€0.05–€0.15 / conversation) |
    | Voice minutes | Low (forwarded) |
    | **Total** | **€20–€50 / country** |
    
    ---
    
    ## **7️⃣ Scaling Rule (Phase 2)**
    
    You only add more numbers if:
    
    - call volume is very high, **or**
    - you want portal-specific attribution numbers
    
    Even then:
    
    - still **not per property**
    - still resolved via Place ID
    
    ---
    
    ## **8️⃣ Admin Visibility (WF-A4 — Integrations)**
    
    Each country shows:
    
    | **Country** | **Voice** | **SMS** | **WhatsApp** | **Status** | **Last Activity** | **Cost** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | UK | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | Active | 2 min ago | €32 |
    | DE | — | ✅ | ✅ | Active | 6 min ago | €21 |
    
    “➕ Add number” button exists but unused in Phase 1.
    
    ---
    
    ## **🔒 FINAL LOCK — Twilio Numbers**
    
    > NoAgent uses one primary Twilio number per country for voice and SMS, plus one WhatsApp sender.
    > 
    
    > Numbers are generic and never property-specific.
    > 
    
    > Property identification is handled exclusively via Place ID resolution.
    > 
    
    > This keeps costs low, operations simple, and scaling predictable.
    > 
    
    ---
